Indaba yokusakazwa kwemidlalo yamazwe kulapho kuvele khona inkinga kutholakala ukuthi kunemali eningi ekhokhwa ngendlela engaqondile ekubeni amazwe ase - Afrika kungewona wonke ahlomulayo ngalokhu .
Sekungumlando ukuthi indodana ka - Issa Hayatou owayengumengameli weCaf isikhathi eside , ibibalwa kubaphathi benkampani yaseFrance okuyiyona ebiwaphethe wonke amagunya okusakazela i - Caf imidlalo yayo .
Ngenxa yalokhu , imidlalo yeBafana bese kujwayelekile ukuthi uma isekuhambeni ingakhonjiswa kwithelevishini .
Kuyimanje imidlalo yeCaf Champions League neyeConfederations , yamaqembu aseNingizimu Afrika , kayikhonjiswa uma isekuhambeni .
UMotsepe ukholelwa ekutheni uma zingalungiswa zonke lezi zinto , iCaf izohlonishwa emhlabeni .
Izincomo eziphume emihlanganweni elokhu iqale ngoMashi zikhomba ukuthi kufanele ibhekwe indlela okuphathwa ngayo imiqhudelwano kanjalo nendlela abaqashiwe abasebenza ngayo .
Kusemqoka ukuthi kufakwe imali ezinkundleni njengoba kushaywe umthetho othi wonke amazwe angaphansi kweCaf kumele okungenani abe nenkundla eyodwa esezingeni leFifa .
Ubudlelwano obukhona nabaxhasi kumele buqiniswe kakhulu kunakuqala kuphinde kuqashwe abantu abawufundele ngendlela umsebenzi ngokwahlukana kwezinhlaka .
IPatrice Motsepe Foundation isivele ixhase i - Caf Pan - African Schools Football Championship ngo - $ 10 million .
Kusemqoka kuMotsepe ukuthuthukiswa kwebhola labesifazane bese kuqinisekiswa ukuthi isithunzi sonondweba sihloniphekile izwekazi lonke .
Okukhulu kunakho konke uMotsepe akufunayo , ukuqala kokusetshenziswa kwemishini ye - Video Assistant Referee ( VAR ) .
Ukugcizelele ukuthi kumele kuthengwe le eshibhile kodwa esebenza kahle , hhayi le emba eqolo ekubeni izokwenza umsebenzi ofanayo .
Ngempelasonto edlule , kubonakale kusebenza okokuqala iVAR emidlalweni eyandulela owamanqamu yeChampions League .
UHunt uzibona ekhuza ibuya maduze ekuqeqesheni
ANGASE abonakale maduze ebhentshini uGavin Hunt osanda kuxoshwa yiKaizer Chiefs yize eyibeke kowandulela owamanqamu weCaf Champions League .
UHunt uqashwe iChiefs ekuqaleni kwesizini ethatha izintambo ku - Ernst Middendorp okuyisinqumo esenze abalandeli bayo babuyelwa yithemba ngeqembu labo kwazise belihlehla nyova .
Kusobala - ke nokho ukuthi izinto azizange zihambe kahle ngaphansi kobuholi bukaHunt yize iChiefs ibingavumelekile ukuthenga abadlali ( ngesikhathi sakhe ) .
Ukuhlulwa kweChiefs yiBlack Leopards ngoMeyi 26 yikhona okuphoqe Amakhosi ukuthi athathe isinqumo sokulihlukanisa ifindo leminyaka emithathu noHunt .
Kuliqiniso ukuthi izinto azizange zimvume lo mqeqeshi kwiChiefs yize enomlando wokudla izicoco .
IChiefs imfaka amasondo nje isaphumelele ukuwina imidlalo emibili kwengu - 17 yeligi ilandelana .
Ukufaka iChiefs kweyandulela owamanqamu kwiChampions League akuzange kumsize uHunt ogcine exoshwa okokuqala empilweni yakhe yokuqeqesha esigabeni esikhokhelayo eNingizimu Afrika .
Ethintwa Isolezwe izolo emini uHunt uthe , yize engathandi ukukhuluma ngosekudlule kodwa ngeke afihle ukuthi ucabanga ngonobhutshuzwayo ubusuku nemini .
" Ngabe ngiqamba aluhlaza uma ngingathi ngiyalijabulela leli khefu engilitholile emuva kweminyaka eminingi .
Ngicabanga ngonobhutshuzwayo ubusuku nemini .
Nakuthelevishini ayikho enye into engiyibukayo ngaphandle kwebhola .
Ngisho elakudala yinqobo nje uma kungunobhutshuzwayo , " kusho uHunt .
Ebuzwa ngokuthi kungalindeleka nini ukuthi abonakale ebhentshini uthe , ukuphela kwesizini yikhona okuzocacisa okuningi .
" Kuhle ngoba isizini isizophela .
Kulapho izinto eziningi ezizokwenzeka khona .
" Angikwazi ukusho okuzokwenzeka kodwa isikhathi yisona esizocacisa ngekusasa lami .
Ngeke ngithathe ikhefu njengoba behlale benza abanye abaqeqeshi kodwa okuningi kuzocaca ngami maduze , " kusonga uHunt .
Uthe akafuni ukukhuluma ngokusekudlulile .
Akhona amaqembu asemataniswa noHunt selokhu exoshiwe .
Phakathi kwamaqembu akhonjwa kuwona kubalwa iStellenbosch FC neSuperSport United .
La maqembu aphekwa uSteve Barker noKaitano Tembo ngokwahlukana .
Kuthiwa iSuperSport izimisele ngokubuyisa uHunt oyakhele udumo edla izicoco eminyakeni edlule .
Imbangela yalokhu ukungenami kwayo ngokugcwele ngoTembo .
Kuyavela nokuthi iStellies okuyiqembu langakubo uHunt kwazise ungowaseKapa , iyamnyonyobela kodwa konke kuncike ekutheni iyalivika yini izembe ebhekene nalo .
Qaphela uma kuthiwa thwasa ukuze ungazifaki enkingeni
KWENZEKE umhlola kufika izelamani zogogo abathathu asebengaphezulu kweminyaka engu - 60 , nezingane zabo nabazukulu bekhala izinyembezi ngamunye ngamunye esigodlweni eMlambomunye , bethi indlela abahlupheka ngayo sekuthi abazibulale .
Ngokungena ngokwehlukana ababili bathwasa omunye wasinda yena , ukuthi kanjani naye uyazibuza .
Ekuthwaseni kwabo eminyakeni engu - 20 eyedlule akukho lutho olwaphinde lwalunga .
Kwalowo owabathwasisa akasekho emhlabeni lasheshe lamthatha ithongo lakhe okukhomba kona ukuthi wayedlala ngabantu .
Lezi zalukazi esiganele kwaGumede waseNtshangwe nodadewabo oganele kwaNzama eCato Ridge bobabili bakhala ezimathonsi ngenxa yenhlupheko esibapheke iminyaka engaphezu kuka - 20 selokhu bathwasa .
Omunye wabo kwathi angaphothula zashona zonke izingane zakhe kwasala eyodwa nayo esinomzukulu okungathi uphithanelwa yikhanda .
Ugogo uNzama yena indodakazi yakhe ngenhlanhla yagana kodwa nayo yathwasiswa , ekuthwaseni kwayo yathi iqeda umkhwenyana wayekhala iphepha .
Kumanje ilahlekelwe ngumsebenzi .
Kanti phambilini beyiwuthola umsebenzi kodwa usheshe uphele .
Bafika eMlambomunye belandelana ngenxa yenhlupheko nosizo asebethe banikezwa lona kuba nhlanga zimuka nomoya .
Ugogo uGumede yena useke waya komunye wathi akalethe inkomo emhlophe khona ezomvulela idlozi , uma ebuza ukuthi uzoyithathaphi imali wathi akahambe ayoyiboleka ngoba idlozi lakhe lavalwa .
Uma ubuza ngodadewabo naye owathwasa njengaye , impendulo ithi udadewabo bamvala ngezizwe kufanale yena akhiphe imali engangezinkulungwane ezingu - 50 zamaRandi ukuze ayomlahla izizwe bese emgeza emfuleni ongcolile ukuze zihambe nokungcola .
Bobabili bakhala ngokuthi abasazazi izingubo asebazishiya emifuleni bebhabazwa ngezinkukhu ngoba kuthiwa bakhishwa idlozi elibi abalifakwa ugobela owayebathwasisa .
Yilezi zimangaliso engihlale ngikhuluma ngazo ngithi baningi abantu abathwasile kodwa akwenzeki lutho .
Abanye baba nenhlanhla yokuthi batshelwe ukuthi phuma lapha kudlalwa ngathi .
Izingane eziningi namhlanje ezifundayo ezehluleka ezikoleni kokunye zilahlekelwe ngumsebenzi ngenxa yendaba eba yisiphetho yokuthi akuthwaswe .
Engiqonde namhlanje ukudlulisela kuwona wonke umuntu wukuthi ngo - 2021 , ake ubalekele kude nale Covid yokuthwasiswa kwabantu kungekho sidingo .
Leli gama nalesi senzo ake kufane nesihogo esizokushisa uma ungene ungaboni .
Bakhona okufanele bathwase kodwa nazi izinto okufanele ziqikelelwe : izibonakaliso namaphupho ikhona okungumnqamulajuqu ekuthwaseni .
Ukuphupha amabhayi namashoba nokuzibona ugida nezangoma , nokugula , ngake ngabhala khona lapha ngisho ukuthi yebo kusuke kukhomba ukuthi yamukela umsebenzi kodwa kufanele kube abanikazi bawo okufanele bakukhombe kumuntu ozoya kuyena kumbe bazozenzela .
Kunezinkulumo eziningi lapha ngaphandle kithina belaphi okuphika ukuthi ithongo liyakwazi ukuzenzela konke , imbangela yalokho ingoba asazi futhi sisenolwazi oluncane ngethongo nedlozi , nabathi bayalazi basuke bekhulumela emadwaleni olwazi olungaphelele .
Yinto yokucwaningwa kabanzi lena nokuzinika isineke futhi iphinde ibe ukuphathiswa kwakho , hhayi ukuzenzela .
Ngakho baningi abantu abathintwe ngempade okungeyona , umuntu kuthi kudingeka ukuba adle impande yomndawe kodwa anikwe impande yesiNguni .
Lezi zinto azihlangani .
Kukhona lapho ithongo lifuna izandla zowesifazane , kodwa usukeleke owesilisa akuthwasise , noma lifuna owesilisa owesifazane akuthwasise kuxabane konke .
Okukhulu wukuthi unayo yini leyo mpande efanele edingwa yidlozi noma yithongo lalowo muntu ? Okogogo bobabili , emndenini wangakubo kanina kwakukhona isalukazi esathwasa emanzini esingukhokho wonina esivela siyisizukulwane sesihlanu saphuma nenyoka nezikhwana khona emanzini .
Lesi salukazi sasithwele abalozi ngqo , okwahamba sashona naso .
Akuphindanga kwaba khona okuvela kuyena kobunyanga .
Manje sesibuya ngalaba bazukulu , kodwa ukubuya kwaso sesibuya njengemimoya yeNdiki , okufanele sigezwe kubona .
Inkinga ukuthi ekugezweni kwabo kufanele bagezwe ngegazi lengwe , namaphakama amhlophe edlozi lomndawe , atholakala eMozambique kuphela .
Kulapho - ke ogobela belahleke khona base bebona ithuba lokuthwasisa izalukazi .
Izigodlo eziningi uma ubuza impande ezisebenza ngayo kunzima , uthola ukuthi sithenga sonke khona laphaya eZimbuzini , kumbe koBerea , umuntu akakaze angene ngisho ehlathini ayoyibona ngamehlo impande imbiwa , namaphakama ukuthi akhiwa kanjani ehlathini .
Kokunye uphathisiwe yini leyo mpande nokuthi ukuphathiswa kwakho kwedlozi kuluhlobo luni ?
Abantu abaningi bahlushwa idlozi lomndawe iningi lethu elithi siyakwazi ukulisebenza kanti libi ngokuthanda ukuzenzela .
Ngakho qaphela , uma kuthiwa thwasa phakamisa izindlebe namakhala njengenyamazane , ngoba ayikho into ebuhlungu njengokuthi uhlupheke uze uyofa ngisho nesizukulwane sakho ngoba wenza okungekona .
Owakwenzisa uyobe engasekho uyobe ususele wedwa nezingane nesizukulwane sakho .

Imfundo yethu kumele ibe nobunkipha bukoloni
IZIFUNDISWA ezimnyama futhi eziqavile zisakhala ngokuthi ulwazi olukhiqizwa emanyuvesi ase - Afrika , kumele luguqulwe lufane nolwabantu abamnyama abafundiswa khona .
USolwazi Pikita Ntuli wake waphawula kwithelevishini ngokuthi amanyuvesi e - Afrika , ngokwezakhiwo akhona kodwa amanyuvesi obu - Afrika ngokwesiko - mpilo owekho eNingizimu Afrika .
Amanyuvesi obu - Afrika kumele akhombise futhi aphakamise isiko - mpilo lase - Afrika emfundweni nasekuhlelweni kwawo .
Amanyuvesi obu - Afrika yiwo okumele akhiqize ulwazi nocwaningo oluqhakambisa ubu - Afrika kodwa ngeshwa awamaningi .
Amanyuvesi obu - Afrika kumele aphinde akhiqize ulwazi oluzolekelela ekuguqulweni kwezimo mqondo ezimbi ngezwekazi lethu , i - Afrika .
Akumele sibe namanyuvesi ase - Afrika kuphela .
Kumele sibe namanyuvesi obu - Afrika .
Izifundiswa ezimnyama okumele zenze lowo msebenzi azibonwa nangokhalo .
Amanyuvesi e - Afrika okumele abe izizinda zokukhiqiza ulwazi afukanyelwe izifundiswa ezimpisholo ngokwebala kodwa ezivikela noma eziphatha isiko - mpilo laseNtshonalanga , njengezikhali zamaNtungwa .
Isiko - mpilo laseNtshonalanga luvikelwa ngokuthi ulwazi olukhiqizwa kulezi zikhungo zemfundo ephakeme lunika udumo nenhlonipho kwizindlela zokucabanga nezokuphila zaseNtshonalanga .
Izindlela zase - Afrika zokucabanga nezokuphila zivezwa njengezidelelekile nezingabalulekile .
Kuyiqiniso elingephikwe ukuthi eNingizimu Afrika nase - Afrika jikelele , zisashoda kakhulu izifundiswa ezimnyama ezicabanga ngendlela yobu - Afrika emikhiqizweni yolwazi , phecelezi ucwaningo .
Singakusho kugcwale umlomo ukuthi ubuso balezi zifundiswa bumnyama bhuqe kodwa izimo - mqondo zazo zimhlophe .
Injulalwazi uLious Althusser yake yabuza umbuzo onohlonze .
Yabuza ukuthi : " Yini efundwa izingane esikoleni ? "
Lowo mbuzo usabalulekile nanamhlanje .
Lombuzo ubaluleke ngoba lokho okufundiswa izingane ezikoleni kunomthelela omkhulu endleleni ingane noma umuntu azibona ngayo .
UKarl Marx , wake wathi : " Laba abasemandleni ngokomnotho ezweni yibona abalawula imfundo nesiko - mpilo lesizwe .
" Imfundo evuna ukubukelwa phansi kwabantu abamnyama idala ukuzibukela phansi ezinganeni .
Imfundo yethu eqinisweni isavuna abaseNtshonalanga njengesizinda sodwana sobuhlakani .
Ngoba njengokusho kukaMarx abasemandleni ( abamhlophe ) , balawula ulwazi olukhiqhizwayo nolubonwa njengolubalulekile ezweni .
Kuzomele sizinuke amakhwapha sihlaziyisise ukuthi lemfundo esiyitholayo iyasisondeza yini na kubuthina njengama - Afrika ?
Noma ilekelela kwisimo - mpilo elidume umhlaba wonke lokungathandwa kwethu njengabantu abampisholo .
Kungani iChina elifundile lingalahlekelwa ubuChina balo ?
Kanye neNgisi elifundile alilahlekelwa ubuNgisi balo .
Yithina kuphela abantu bendlu emnyama abafunda babuye badedele okwabo .
Izifundiswa ezimnyama emanyuvesi zithi kumele kube ne - Decolonization ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme .
Igama elikhulu futhi elisematheni kulezi zinsuku .
Konje yini uku - decolonizer ngesiZulu ?
Kunzima ukuphendula lombuzo ngoba izifundswa zethu ezimnyama azikukhathaleli ukuchaza izinto ngolimi abantu abalizwayo .
Ngakho - ke , amagama esintu anaba ngalezingxoxo mpikiswano ebantwini ngolimi lwabo awekho .
Kunamampunge asabalele ngamandla okuthi ukufunda kangcono nokuhlakanipha ukukwazi ukukhuluma isiNgisi kahle .
IsiNgisi esihle futhi esikhulu asichazi ukuthi uhlakaniphe kangcono .
Kumele sishintshe indlela esicabanga ngayo .
Siziqhenye ngobuthina nezilimi zethu .
Uku - decolonizer , abanye bakubiza ngenkipha bukoloni .
Le nkipha bukoloni ichaza ukuthi njengabantu abamnyama kumele sizikhulule emakhamandeleni ezindlela zolwazi lwaseNtshonalanga .
Singavumi ukuthi abaseNtshonalanga basihambele phambili ekulobeni ngesiko - mpilo lwethu .
Ukuhanjelwa phambi njalo ngabaseNtshonalanga kufakazelwa indlela umlando wethu olotshwe ngayo .
Kungani umlando wethu oqukethwe emanyuvesi ukhiqizwe solwazi abamhlophe abanye abaphesheya ?
Yihlazo lelo !
Kucace bha ukuthi lezo zifundiswa ezimhlophe ngeke zilande kahle ngomlando wethu .

Sizimisele ukufaka igxalaba ukulwa nesitha esingabonakali
NGENKATHI uNobhala - Jikelele weNhlangano yezeMpilo eMhlabeni , uDkt Tedros Ghebeyesus , etshela umhlaba ukuthi umkhuhlane iCovid 19 usuthathwa njengombhedukazwe lokho kwakhomba ngokosobala ukuthi njengezwe nesifundazwe kumele sonke sibambe iqhaza ngokubambisana ekulweni nesitha esingabonakali kodwa esiqhubekayo
nokubhuqabhuqa abantu emhlabeni .
Ukulwa nokubhebhetheka komkhuhlane iCorona akubanga kusaba yinto ebhekene noMnyango wezeMpilo kepha yonke iminyango kahulumeni kwadinga ibe yimbumba zimpondo zonke ukweqela ukubhebhetheka kwegciwane .
Ukuba kwethu emkhakheni wokwakha eMnyangweni wezokuHlaliswa kwaBantu neMisebenzi yoMphakathi kusenze saba sophondweni lwempi yokulwa neCovid 19 .
Ngenxa yokuba kulo mnyango sibe sesijutshwa ukuthi sithole izindawo ezifanele zokugonqa ezizosetshenziswa wuMnyango wezeMpilo kuzo zonke izifunda eziwu - 11 zesifundazwe .
Sikwenzile - ke lokho ngokushesha sazithola izindawo nezakhiwo zikahulumeni eziqintile okubalwa kuzo izikole ezingasasebenzi ngoba zavalwa ngenxa yokwehla kwesibalo sabafundi ababebhalisele ukufunda kuzo .
Ukwengezela kulokhu , uMnyango wezeMisebenzi yoMphakathi usebenzisa uhlelo lwawo loMklamo weMisebenzi yoMphakathi eYandisiwe , phecelezi i - EPWP ,
enikezele ngesibalo esiphezulu samavolontiya azobe ehamba phambili emkhankasweni wokufutha ngesibulalimagciwane ezindaweni eziyizakhiwo nemijondolo nakolindela nakumaCommunity Residential Units , lokhu esasikubiza ngamahostela phambilini .
Lo mkhankaso unganyelwe wuMnyango wezokuHlaliswa kwaBantu .
Siwethule ekuqaleni kwesonto komasispala baseMandeni ( eNyoni ) , esifundeni Ilembe nasezakhiweni zakwaJika Joe , Merrivale , nakwaSaicca eMkhondeni kuMasipala waseMsunduzi esifundeni uMgungundlovu .
Emva kokuba uhulumeni omkhulu ememezele isimo senhlekelele kuzwelonke , isigungu esikhulu sesifundazwe sijube uMnyango wezokuHlaliswa kwaBantu ukuthi uqale ngokushesha umkhankaso wokufutha ngesibulalimagciwane ezindaweni eziyizakhiwo nemijondolo ngoba zisengcupheni yokubhebhethekisa umkhuhlane ngenxa yokuba yisidlavela .
Inhlosongqangi yohlelo lokufutha wukuzama ukunqanda ukubhebhetheka nokungena kwegciwane iCorona ezindaweni zokuhlala eziyisidlavela ezifana nazo izakhiwo noma imijondolo , kolindela nasemahostela .
Uhlelo lokufutha ngesibulalimagciwane kumanje seluqalile kuzo zonke izifunda okubalwa kuzo noMasipala waseThekwini nakubo bonke omasipala abanezakhiwo noma imijondolo nezindawo ezingolindela .
UMasipala waseThekwini unezindawo eziningi ezinemijondolo noma izakhiwo ezingolindela .
Sithathe isinqumo sokuthi umkhankaso sizowenza ngohlelo lwe - Operation Sukuma Sakhe lapho bonke ongqongqoshe abangoShampeni be - Operation Sukuma Sakhe ezifundeni kuzoba yibo abahola umkhankaso ozobe ubheke ngqo komasipala abanezakhiwo eziyimijondolo , olindela namahostela .
Ngaphezu kokuthi sizofutha ngesibulalimagciwane , uMnyango wezokuHlaliswa kwaBantu uthenge insipho yokugeza izandla noketshezi lokuhlanza izandla okuzonikezwa umphakathi lapho uhlelo lokufutha ngesibulalimagciwane luzobe lwenziwa khona .
Ukufika kombhedukazwe kusinike ithuba nathi siwuhulumeni ukuthi sifundise abantu bakithi ngezempilo eziyisekelo zansuku zonke njengokuthi kumele kugezwe izandla ngokuphindelela ngamanzi nensipho nanokuthi abantu bakithi baqikelele ukuthi izindawo abahlala kuzo zihlale zihlanzekile ukuze amagciwane angakwazi ukwakhela kuzo .
Siphinde futhi sifundise abantu ukuthi bajwayele ukuzivocavoca ukuze imizimba ingabi ntekenteke .
Lokhu bangakwenza khona lapho behlala khona ngoba akukhuthazwa ukuthi babe nguvanzi emgwaqweni .
Siphinde futhi sibanxuse ukuthi ngazo zonke izikhathi baqikelele ukuthi bahlala ngokugqagqana ibanga elingangemitha elilodwa ukusuka kumuntu oseduze naye ukuze sigweme ukuthelelana .
Ngokubambisana neminye iminyango kahulumeni wesifundazwe sinalo ithemba ukuthi nathi siwuMnyango wezokuHlaliswa kwaBantu neMisebenzi yoMphakathi sizoqhubeka nokufaka igxalaba ekufuqeni inqola yempi elwa nesitha esingabonakali ukuze ekugcineni sisinqobe .

AbeRET mabashiye i - ANC bakhe iqembu labo
MHLELI : Ake ngiphawule ngesigungu esiphezulu se - ANC esaziwa ngokuthi yiNEC nesinqumo saso sokucela abashushiswayo ngamacala enkohlakalo ukuba bazishenxele bona ezikhundleni noma baphoqwe ukuba bamiswe .
Lesi sinqumo ngisishayela ihlombe .
Sazi sonke ukuthi asizikhetheli abaholi kodwa sibhalelwa uhlu lwabazokhethwa .
Umbuzo wami uthi wubani lo mbhali walolu luhlu na ? Kungani abaholi behamba bethi bakhethwe ngamagatsha ekubeni bezazi abakhethwanga ngamagatsha ?
Akubuyiselwe amandla emagatsheni , ngikhuluma nje sinezimeya ezakhethwa wosomabhizinisi ngoba betshala imali yabo ukuze bahlomule amathenda .
Akungethusi ukufika kwenye yezimeya ehhovozi yathi kumakhansela sekuyisikhathi sensambatheka yento ebizwa ngeRadical Economic Transformation ( RET ) kanti kuzokwebiwa kusetshenziswa itemu leRET .
Uma kungaphenywa ukuthi liqhamukaphi leli temu , ungathola ukuthi lasungulwa yiwo amaGupta lawa ngenhloso yokweba imali yethu eNingizimu Afrika .
Awasekho ke manje amaGupta , ashaye achitha nezikhwama zawo ezazishushunjiswa emagatsheni ukuze kukhethwe abaholi abafunwa yiwo .
Yisikhathi senhlangano ukubuyisa uzinzo embuthweni .
Masethembe , emuva kwesinqumo seNEC , akekho osezonqatshelwa ubulungu .
Manje ngikhuluma nje , kunqantshelwe abantu abangaphezu kwamakhulu amathathu ubulungu eWard 78 ngoba kuhloswe ukubambelela emandleni okuphatha .
Kunjena nje embuthweni , kwavunyelwa abaqoli bazicebisa nemindeni yabo , kumanje imizi yabo ungafunga ukuthi yizigodlo zobukhosi thizeni .
Okumangazayo , kukhona abakujabulelayo lokhu abeRET .
Yisikhathi sabo manje sokuthi baphume iqembu labo lokweba imali yethu , bashiye i - ANC ngokuthula .
Ingamane ilahlekelwe yivoti kunokwebela abakhokhi bentela .
Abahambe basithele !

Yazi kabanzi ngeGEPF ungakathathi umhlalaphansi
UNGQONGQOSHE wezeziMali , uMnuz Tito Mboweni , uphawule ngokuthi uhamba ngonyawo lonwabu umkhankaso kahulumeni wokudedela abasebenzi asebeneminyaka engaphezu kuka - 55 ngesikhathi ethula isabelomali samaphakathi nonyaka ngo - Okthoba .
Akusimangazanga lokho thina esikulo mkhakha wokutshalwa kwemali nokuhlaziya ezomnotho ngoba lolu hlelo salubuka sangakholwa ukuthi lungethulwa luphothulwe esikhathini esifushane kangaka .
Kuningi okwakudingeka kwenzeke ngaphambi kokuba luqale .
Okukhulu ukufundiswa kwamalungu esikhwama sempesheni kahulumeni iGEPF ngenqubomgomo yokuthatha impesheni ngaphambi kwesikhathi .
" Lo mbuzo ukuveze obala ukuthi abafundisiwe kahle abantu .
Kuzokhumbuleka ezifundweni esizethule ezingosini ezedlule ukuthi umuntu osebenza kuhulumeni unezindlela ezintathu zokonga imali yakhe uma eyeka ukusebenza .
Ungathatha imadlana ethile ushiye ingxenye kwiGEPF ezoqhubeka ikuholele inyanga nenyanga uze ufe .
Ungayithatha futhi imali uyifake enkampanini ezimele esiza abafisa ukonga imali yabo ngaphandle kwesamba sikahulumeni sempesheni .
Ungayithatha yonke imali yakho uyifake ebhange bese uzilawula wena ekuyisebenziseni .
Siye sabhala futhi nangobubi nobuhle bazo zonke lezi zindlela esizibalile .
Okunye kwalokho yinhlawulo nezinsiza zokushiya imali kwiGEPF umuntu bese ehola ngenyanga .
Lapho sincome kakhulu uhulumeni ngesamba abhekela ngaso abamsebenzela baze badlule emhlabeni .
Kodwa okungekuhle wukuthi uma umuntu eshona eganiwe noma eganile , imali eholwa umyeni noma unkosikazi iyancipha ngesibalo esingu - 50 % .
Angikuqinisekise ukuthi le mali akuyona imali eholwa ngoba kucatshangelwa izingane kodwa iqondene nabashadile .
Sabuye saxoxa ngokuthi uma kwenzeka ngebhadi beshona kanyekanye abaganene , kulandelwa imigomo kahulumeni yomhlalaphansi .
Ayikho imali yenyanga nenyanga eya emndenini uma beshone beneminyaka engaphezu kuka - 55 futhi kungukuthi sebeneminyaka emihlanu bayeka emsebenzini .
Lesi simo senza baphithane amakhanda abaningi .
Yisona esibavusele umbuzo othi uma nginikezwe imvume yokuthatha umhlalaphansi ongenanhlawulo ngingasihoxisa yini isinqumo sami sokwamukela lesi sinxephezelo ? Siye saxhumana nabakwaGEPF abasichazele ukuthi uma ukhethe i - early retirement usuke usushade nohulumeni impilo yakho yonke .
Lokho besikwazi nathi .
Uma ufisa ukuhlukana nohulumeni ungathatha isamba sakho usiyise enkampanini efana neNkunzi Wealth Group noma kwabanye abazimele , noma uyifake ebhange . Manje umbuzo wokuhoxisa isinqumo sokuguqula uhlelo lokuhamba kwakho uphenduleke kanjani ?
Kuthiwa uma ufisa ukubuyekeza isinqumo sakho ungaxhumana nomnyango wakwandabazabantu ufake isicelo sokumiswa kohlelo " olukushadisa nohulumeni . "
Uma isicelo sakho singakafiki kwaGEPF ePitoli , kungenzeka bamise inqubo yalo mshado bese ufaka incwadi kabusha yokwesula .
Kubalulekile ukuthola ulwazi olunzulu ngoba kuningi ukuphambana kwemibono ngisho nakhona kwaGEPF .
Sikhuthaza abanemibuzo ukuba basithinte noma bathinte abakwaGEPF ukuze bachazeleke kahle .

Ngiyalwesaba usizi oluza nobuchwepheshe be - 4IR
MHLELI : Ngibona kuyisikhathi sokuba sivule amehlo njengoba kungena ubuchwepheshe obubizwa ngeFourth Industrial Revolution ( 4IR ) lapho izinto eziningi zizokwenziwa yimishini .
Ukuba kuya ngami ngabe manje sesiyabona ukuthi kwakubalulekile ukufunda kwabadala senze izinto njengabo .
Ngibona abantu abaningi bezophelelwa yimisebenzi ngenxa yokuthi lo mshini obizwa ngerobhothi ukwazi ukwenza imisebenzi yabantu abayishumi uwodwa ngehora elilodwa .
Kuhle sibuyele kwesasikwenza emandulo silime sifuye ngoba bengibuka eminye yemishini ezofakwa ezimayini uma kumbiwa phansi .
Umshini ngamunye uqondiswa abantu ababili wenze umsebenzi owenziwa abasebenzi abaningi .
Lokhu ukwenza ngamahora ambalwa .
Kukhona nerobhothi okuthiwa lizonikeza abantu ukudla ezindaweni zokudla .
Bantu bakithi masingawudeleli umnotho womhlabathi nemfuyo ngoba luyeza usizi lobubha komnyama .
Lokhu esinakho masingakulahli ngoba akuthina sonke esifundile esiyomelana nalesi simo sosizi esizayo .
Osafunda ukuba kuya ngami ngabe ufundela ukuba le mpi imfice esehlome ngazo zonke izikhali zemfundo kuthi ongakwazanga ukuthola ithuba lemfundo aqinise kokumenza aphile kahle nomndeni wakhe .
Ikhwelo likaShenge alilalelwe esaphefumula
MHLELI : Ukubuyisana phakathi kwezinhlangano zombusazwe kubalulekile ngoba ukungezwani kuvimba indlela eya phambili .
UMntwana waKwaPhindangene , kade ayelishumayeli leli vangeli lokukhumelana umlotha .
Yebo kona baningi abadlula ngezikhathi zodlame kwi - IFP ne - ANC kodwa kumele impilo iqhubeke kwabasele ukuze kugwenywe isimo singaphinde senzeke .
Owaba ngumengameli wokuqala wentando yabantu , uMnuz Nelson Mandela , emhlanganweni wokuqala ephumile ejele wathi makube noxolo izikhali ziphonswe olwandle .
Abenhlangano yakhe bavuka umbhejazana kwathiwa ubulawa ukuguga .
Kulapho uMadiba abona khona ukuthi abantu ababenobuntu engakagwetshwa babengasekho .
Ababesekhaleni yibona futhi abaKwaZulu - Natal asebengabaholi namhlanje .
Akusikho ukuthi uMadiba uze wahamba emhlabeni engasiboni isidingo kodwa ubengaphansi kwengcindezi .
Ukhombisile ngendlela abekhonze ngayo ubuholi bukaShenge ngokumbambisa isikhundla sokuba umengameli wezwe uma ephumile eNingizimu Afrika .
Ayekwenza kwakungehli kahle kosomathuba be - ANC .
Wabamba elikhulu iqhaza ewuma emphinjeni umbuso wobadlululo ; kukhona lapho owayengumengameli wombuso wobandlululo uMnuz P W Botha afuna ukuhlangana nabaholi abangawuthathanga uzimele geqe uMntwana wanqaba ukuya kulowo mhlangano .
Wathi ngeke aye engakakhululwa uMadiba nayegqunywe nabo ejele kuphinde kubuye abasekudingisweni .
Lokhu kwenzeke ngeminyaka yawo - 1980 .
UBotha waze wathi uShenge uzenza inkunzi ekhonyayo kwezinye esibayeni .
Nango - 1976 owabe eyimeya yaseSundumbili , eMandeni , uMnuz Gcaleka namakhansela angaphansi kwakhe bamnika inkululeko yaseMandeni , eSundumbili .

Asihalalisele uKhuba siyeke umona
MHLELI : Uyazi angazi ukuthi abanye abantu badalwa kanjani , abakwazi ukubongela omunye umuntu uma enze kahle bafuna izinto abangazisho ezingazama ukuvala leyo mpumelelo yakhe , abantu banomona .
Balandeli bakamaskandi kungenina nonke njalo kepha ngoba izinkulumo ezingamampunge ziphuma kuwona la maqoqo omaskandi koFacebook kuthukwa abaculi amagama abo ehudulelwa phansi .

Uma kuwuthi lokho kuyakuhlula awumfuni , thula phela musa ukudumisa amanga umdala .
Nithe uzivotele , nathi usizwe uKhathide " Tshatha " Ngobe , nathi ugwazele Ukhozi FM .
Kahle hle la mavoti awugabagaba angaka aniboni ukuthi abaculi ayebhekene nabo ubashaye wabaphindaphinda .

Luyinkinga uthando olwakhiwe ngomuthi
Distance GumedeNGIYAZI ukuthi singabantu senza izinto ngendlela engafani futhi sicabanga ngokungafani , kodwa ngiyafisa abantu bazijwayeze ukungayifaki imithi othandweni ngoba uthando olunomuthi phakathi aluphili kahle .
Akukhathaleki kungabe usetshenziswa owesifazane okanye owesilisa .
Namhlanje ngifisa ukukhuluma nabantu abakhonze kakhulu ukusebenzisa imithi ukuze baqinise uthando noma ukuze benze uthando lusebenze .
Okokuqala kumele nazi ukuthi uthando umuzwa ozifikela wona akusiyo into ongayakha noma ongayiphoqa , yebo ngiyavuma ikhona imithi yokwakha uthando kodwa imvamisa lolo thando alupheli kahle ngoba kusuke kuwuthando lokuzakhela .
Uthando olwakhiwe ngomuthi luba nezinkinga eziningi ngokuhamba kwesikhathi kokunye uthole ukuthi awusenayo imali yokulanda umuthi bese kuyaqala kuyamosheka okanye uthole ukuthi obumsebenzisela umuthi sebemvusile waphaphama umuthi awusazweli .
Ngaphandle kokuthi umuntu osetshenziselwe umuthi ugcina esedansela esakho isigingci kodwa buningi ubungozi obungadalwa umuthi kuloyo muntu , okungaba ukuthi omunye uyamgulisa mhlawumbe aze ashone ngenxa yedliso , omunye umenze aphathwe isifuba esingapheli , omunye umphendule isilwane ngisho uthi uyochama afune ukuhamba nawe .
Ngisho uya emcimbini ekhaya kini afune ukuhamba nawe agcine esekulusa engasafuni ngisho ubingelelwe abantu , isigcino akushaye uma ebona uhambisana nomuntu wobulili obungafani nobakho bese ekugcineni athi kungcono sife sobabili ngoba nginomona ngawe angifuni muntu eduze kwakho .
Kuningi nokunye okungaba ingozi othandweni olwakhiwe ngomuthi , yingakho kubalulekile ukuzifundisa ukuthanda ngenhliziyo yakho nangothando olusuka ekujuleni , uma seluphelile futhi ungaphoqi isimo kodwa wamukele bese uqhubeka nempilo yakho .
Ngiyazi sikhuluma nje baningi abantu abazitshela ukuthi basothandweni kanti olwamanga futhi lusazophela , ngiyafisa nalabo abazinikele ekwakheni uthando ngomuthi kube ukuthi sebeyayazi into abayifunayo nabayenzayo ngoba kubuhlungu ukudlisa ingane yomuntu uyiphendule isithithithi sakho ekugcineni uyilaxaze kanjalo ebese ilokhu ikulandela
ngenxa yokuthi kunale nto owayifaka yona .
Akusilona ke idliso elingena emlonyeni kuphela kodwa ziningi izinto ezenziwa abantu abomele ukuthandwa ngenkani .
Abanye bashiqeka nezinto ezithweni zabo zangasese ukuze babe mnandi ngethemba lokuthi ngeke uthando luphele .
Ngake ngasho ekuqaleni ngathi indoda iyakushiya noma umnandi , ngasho futhi ukuthi uthando lwakhiwa amagatsha amaningi ahlukahlukene , ayikho into eqinisa uthando ukudlula isimilo inhlonipho , ukuxhumana nokuzwana komoya negazi futhi nifane nabangani .
Umuthi ningawufaki othandweni lwenu ngoba uzomosha izinto futhi inhlonipho nokunye kwalokhu engikubale ngenhla kungaqhamuki kumuntu oyedwa kodwa akuqhamuke nhlangothi zombili ngoba phela niyathandana .
Ungazisebenzisela umuthi wakho uma ufuna ukuzihlanza wena ukuze ungabi nesigcwagcwa nakubantu futhi ukuze nezichitho zingangeni kalula kuwena ugcine usunesidina kumuntu wakho kodwa hhayi ukuthi uze uhambe impela uye enyangeni nesikhindi somuntu wakho sangaphansi ngoba uthi ufuna ezwe wena wedwa okanye induku ivuke uma elele nawe
wedwa okanye uma nje eke wakhulunyiswa yindoda ethi iyamshela avele angene esikhathini ngokushesha .
Lezo zinto ziyingozi ngoba zenza uhlale ungenamali kwazise phela wena usebenzela ukuthenga umuthi futhi zenza uthando luphele kabuhlungu impela .
Asisebenzeni ngothando olukhona sikhohlwe olomuthi ngoba luchitha nesikhathi lunjalo nje .
I - NFP isalidinga ithuba lokukhombisa ubuqotho
MHLELI : ENingizimu Afrika angeke ukhulume ngepolitiki ungayibali iNFP noMengameli wayo uNkk Zanele Magwaza - Msibi uyathanda awuthandi .
Ukusungulwa kwaleli qembu kwavula ikhasi elisha kwipolitiki yaseNingizimu Afrika okwaba yiqembu lokuqala elathi lifika leza nokuhlukile okusha ebalazweni lepolitiki yaseNingizimu Afrika .
I - NFP iyiqembu lokuqala ukuphakamisa ukuthi abafundi abaphume ku - matric sebenezincwadi zokushayela mahhala , iNFP ingamavulandlela ngohlelo lwezolimo nokuxhasa imiphakathi ngogandaganda njengoba bonke omasipala sebekwenza , ukunakekela abangenabani .
Kumele siwazise umphakathi waseNingizimu Afrika lelo qiniso .
Siyiqembu lokuqala ukuveza singafihli ukuhlonipha ubuholi bomdabu amakhosi nezinduna nokuhlonipha iqhaza labo emiphakathini yasemakhaya .
Ukuqoqa okungenhla siyiqembu elikhuluma ngezinto ezithinta abantu ngqo , asikhulumi ngemilingo eshiwo ngabanye uma bekhankasa .
Phezu kwazo zonke izinselelo esesibe nazo njengeqembu kusuka ngo - 2014 kuhlabeka umengameli wethu ngokugula , 2016 sangangena okhethweni lwemikhandlu , kube wu - 2017 abanye abazibiza ngabaholi befaka iqembu enkantolo kwaze kwazaleka ubambimbiswano ngomyalelo wenkantolo olwalubizwa nge - INEC noma Interim National Executive Committe eyasiyisa
engqungqutheleni ngoDisemba 2019 .
Siyababonga nabaholi ababeyibambe lapho kuze kube manje .
Nakulo nyaka uphindile futhi uMlotshwa nahambisaba nabo basifaka enkantolo bethi ababazi ubuholi beqembu .
Uma besho nakulokhu amalungu eNFP asathembekile siyabonga kakhulu sengingasho ngithi sekuyantwela ezansi maduze nje leya NFP yango - 2011 izobuya uma sekuhambe ababulali bayo . Zithembe NgobeseEnquthu
Kumqoka ukuthembana uma silwa nobhubhane
MHLELI : Ngithanda ukudlulisa umbono wami ngomgomo weCovid - 19 .
Sekusuke enkulu inkulumo mpikiswano ngendaba yomgomo weCoronavirus .
Uhulumeni wakithi akakaphawuli ngalokhu .
Kuningi abantu abakushoyo ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngendaba yamakhambi okuvikela nokwelapha iCoronavirus .
Yize singakugqugquzeli ukuthi uhulumeni aphendule yonke into eshiwo ezinkundleni zokuxhumana , lokhu sibona sengathi kumele angenelele eze nezincazelo ezizogculisa isizwe ngale mishanguzo .
Abantu abaningi abanakho ukucaciseleka kahle ngamakhambi okuzivikela nawokwelapha izifo .
Abanye baye babone kufana .
Lokhu - ke kunobungozi ngoba uma uhulumeni engabacaciseli , ngeke banqabe ukugonywa kuphela , bazogcina sebenqaba namakhambi okwelapha .
Lokhu kuyosibeka kwenkulu inkinga ngoba kuyoba nzima ukusiza abantu abangasathembi lutho eqhamuka ezibhedlela ezelapha lesi sifo .
Kuzogcina sekunzima nokufundisa abantu ngalesi sifo uma sebeze bakholwa wukuthi lesi isifo ngesakhiwe .
Njengamanje iNingizimu Afrika iyingxenye yamazwe enza ucwaningo ngamakhambi amane okungenzeka alaphe lesi sifo .
Lolu cwaningo olwaziwa ngeSolidarity Trial luholwa yiNhlangano yezeMpilo eMhlabeni jikelele .
Lolu cwaningo lufake la makhambi : Remdesivir , Chloroquine noma Hydroxy Chloroquine , Lopinavir neRitonavir , Lopinavir ehamba neRitonavir kanye ne - InterferonBeta - 1a .
Lolu cwaningo lwenziwa emazweni amaningi ehlukene , kumele uhulumeni abachazele kabanzi ngalo abantu ukuze kungabi bikho ukusola .
Uma siqhubeka kanje , abanye bazogcina bewenqaba nawo la makhambi yize kunobufakazi bokuthi ayasebenza .
Ubungozi obukhulu obukhona , ngobokuthi noma angatholakala amakhambi okuzivikela kulesi sifo , kuyoba nzima ukugculisa abantu bakithi ukuthi ngempela leli khambi liyasebenza .
Lokhu kuyobeka ingcindezi enkulu kubasenzi bezempilo , okuyibona okumele banike abantu la makhambi .
Uhulumeni kumele ayicacise le nto , ngoba uma eqhubeka eyiziba izodala umonakalo omukhulu , abantu bazokholwa yilokhu abakuzwa ngalabo abangabambisani nala makhambi .
Abantu bazongamethembi uhulumeni , nakho konke akushoyo .
Leli yithuba lokuba abaholi bafundise abantu ngocwaningo olwenzekayo emhlabeni ngalesi sifo , bese beyaveza ukuthi lusithinta kanjani thina lolu cwaningo .
Uma silwa nobhubhane , kubaluleke kakhulu ukuthembana . Sanele NgcoboEPITOLI
Othandweni sekwaba semfuleni wegazi
MHLELI : Namuhla ukuzinikela kumuntu ngenhloso yokumthanda sekufana nokuzinikela ekufeni ngoba awazi azokwenza khona mhla ungahambisani naye .
Emandulo uthando kwakuyinkundla yentokozo kodwa manje sekwaba yinkundla yegazi lapho kuqedwa khona abesifazane kade betshelwe ukuthi bayathandwa .
Amadoda anonya asaphendula uthando udobo lokudoba abesifazane ukuze basondele becabange ukuthi bayathandwa kanti bazokwenzakaliswa .
Sesisaba nokuthembeka kwabesifazane sibakhombise ubumqoka babo ngoba abanye balinyazwe ngabantu ekade bekhuluma njengathi bezenza qotho kanti bafihle ubulwane kubo .
Izingane zethu sezisaba ngisho ukudlala emnyango ngoba nebesithi umalume uzwa kuthiwa udlwengule ingane maqede wayibulala , obani ubulwane madoda ? Ngibhala lo mbhalo ngihlengezela izinyembezi uma ngicabanga ngezimbali zezwe ezibulelwe kujeziswa ukuthi azinamandla .

abesifazane bebala elimhlophe nabo bathuka izanya ngenxa yamadoda anonya ehlangene nabathakathi abazibiza ngezinyanga .

Amaphoyisa aqhwaga abantu imizi yabo eMlaza
MHLELI : Ngithi ake ngidlulise kwelakho iphephandaba ngezinkinga nenkohlakalo okusihlasele eMlaza kodwa abantu bathule sengathi akonakele lutho .

Kunabantu abahamba beqola abantu imizi noma amakhaya .
Ngizokwenzela isibonelo , uma emzini mumbe kungasenabazali kufika lezi zigebengu seziphethe amaphepha omgunyathi .
Zifike zibatshele ukuthi umuzi ngokwemiyalelo yenkantolo usuthengiwe sekuzomele baphume bayofuna indawo yokuhlala .
Babuye bathenjiswe imali encane eyisinxephezelo uma nje bezovuma ukusayina amaphepha okuvuma ukuthi umuzi bayawudedela udayise .
Labo abangavumi kuzofika iqembu labantu lizokhipha ngenkani bashaywe bahlukunyezwe ngazo zonke izindlela zokusabisa .
Lowo muzi uzobe usuphenduka owephoyisa .
Le nto iningi nje eMlaza futhi igcwele kakhulu esigcemeni kwa - U .

Kumanje kunabantu abangazi ukuthi bazolalaphi ngoba imizi yasemakubo isiqhwagwe amaphoyisa aphatha izibhamu imini nobusuku emagcekeni ukuze uma udlula ubone nje ukuthi yimpi yodwa .
Uyazibuza - ke ukuthi iphoyisa elinomuzi walo elawuthenga ngokusemthethweni kwenzeka kanjani lihlale liqalaza egcekeni lihlezi liphethe isibhamu somsebenzi ngesandlaBesicela i - Ipid ingenelele kulolu daba , ikakhulukazi kwa - U ngoba konakele .

Sesifikile isikhathi sokuthi ixoxo nexoxo lizigxumele
MHLELI : Nginesifiso sokubeka uvo lwami mayelana nokusebenza komfelandawonye we - ANC , Cosatu neSACP osufana nento engekho .
Ngicabanga ukuthi sesifikile isikhathi sokuthi inhlangano nenhlangano ithathe isihlalo sayo ukuze ibhekane nezinhloso zayo .
Ngizovuma ukuthi bekunesidingo sokuhlangana kusabhekenwe noMbuso wobandlululo ngoba kwakufanele uhlaselwe ukuze uwe .
Uma sizibheka ngayinye : I - ANC eholwa nguMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa isisembusweni manje futhi ingumqashi ngezindlela ezehlukene nasemazingeni ehlukene .
Abanye abangabaphathi ezinhlakeni zikahulumeni babuye babe nokungayihloniphi imigomo yezabasebenzi ngaleyo ndlela basuke sebephambana nemibono yelungu lomfelandawonye .
ICosatu , ephethwe nguNksz Zingiswa Losi , kumele ihlale esihlalweni sokumela abasebenzi ukuze ibhekane nokumela abasebenzi ngokugcwele .
Njengamanje sinenqwaba yabasebenzi bangaphandle abasebenza kuleli ngokungemthetho .
ICosatu kufanele isebenzisane noMnyango wezaBasebenzi ukubheka ukuthi abaqashi bayahambisana yini nemigomo yokuqashwa kwabasebenzi nokuholelwa kwabo ngokwemigomo kahulumeni .

Kuyo yonke le nto umuntu olimalayo ngumsebenzi oba wumgilwa wobhululu .

Ngabona ukuthi mhlawumbe usekhohliwe wukuthi bebekulabo ababethi uMnuz Jacob Zuma akaphume eMbusweni ngoba unephunga lenkohlakalo .
Ngazibuza ukuthi kanti yini abathi bayigadile uma bezodedela i - ANC ifake abantu abanenkohlakalo .
Nakuba singathi alukapheli nya ubandlululo ezinhlakeni ezithile kodwa kubalulekile ukuthi inhlangano nenhlangano kulezi ezingenhla ibhekane nenhloso eyasungulelwa yona ukuze ifeze injongo nezinkolelo eyasungulwa phezu kwazo .
Njengamanje uhwebo olukhululekile luhlulekile ukuletha impilo engcono kubantu ngobuningi babo emazweni amaningi alandela le nqubo yohwebo olukhululekile okungangokuba amazwe amaningi anezikweletu ezesabekayo amanye awa bhu ngenxa yezikweletu .

Abashenxe omkhulu nogogo ePhalamende badedele intsha
MHLELI : Kwelakho kangisaqondi ukuthi kwenzakani eMzansi .
Ngibona ubaba uSipho Hlomuka eshesha ukungenela komasipala abaphethwe ngamaqembu aphikisayo kodwa abangaphansi kwe - ANC akakwenzi .
Ngabe ubona ukuthi kasimboni yini singabantu ukuthi ufuna ukuzuza omasipala abangekho ngaphansi kwabo .
Mina kangikhali ngoba kangisaboni kwi - ANC ukuthi ukhona ongayebi imali , okanye obhekela obhululu nabasondelene naye .
Uthi wawazi ukuthi indoda ethembeke kangaka , uDkt Zweli Mkhize ingasolwa ngenkohlakalo ? Unenhlanhla yena ngoba ( uMengameli Cyril ) Ramaphosa usalayeza ngokummisa esikhundleni kodwa kuMnuz Ace Magashule wangenela ngokushesha .
Kusobala ukuthi kwayena wubengayilindele le nto yokushenxisa abantu ukuthi ingagadla nakubangani bakhe .
Ngokwami sengathi i - ANC yonke iyasoleka enkohlakalweni .
Kungethusile ukukhishwa kwesibalo sentsha engasebenzi .
Kusobala ukuthi ubugebengu abukazuphela eMzansi ngoba abantu abasha bahleli emakhaya , banesikhathi sonke sokuhlela ubugebengu ukuze baziphilise .
Selokhu kwaphatha i - ANC nje abantu abasha badonsa kanzima .
Kwabona abaholi bazibhekela bona nobhululu babo nemndeni yabo .
Abanye abantu kuya ngokuya badonsa kanzima .
Ake kungakhishwa izibalo zabangasebenzi kodwa kwakhiwe amathuba emsebenzi , basebenze imisebenzi esakhula omkhulu besebenza .
Babengayanga nasesikoleni kungakaphathi i - ANC ?
Sekwanele kwaphatha i - ANC noma kufuneka ozokwakha izindlu zangasese , sekufuneka ono - matric .
Uzibuze ukuthi uzokwenzani u - matric .
Ngisho abasebenza ezitolo sekufuneka wona ngokunjalo nakonogada .
Ngiyafisa kube noshintsho nasePhalamende , kuthi bonke abaneminyaka engaphezu kuka - 60 baphume , kungene intsha engasebenzi , bona bahlale phansi bahole impesheni .
Phumani bantu abadala ePhalamende kungene intsha isebenze .
Mhlawumbe ingaqhamuka namaqhinga amasha , izwe liye phambili .
Izwe limile , kunalokho yinkohlakalo nje okukhulunywa ngayo , ubugebengu , yisifo iCorona neKhomishini kaZondo .
Ukuthi izwe libhekephi mina angiboni kulobu buholi bomkhulu nogogo abagcwele ePhalamende .
Mabashenxe nabo manje bayohlala nemndeni njengabethu ogogo nomkhulu abakhishwa emsebenzini , kwathiwa abayodla impesheni .

Kumele seseke intsha yakuleli futhi siyilalele ukuthi ifunani
NAMHLANJE iNingizimu Afrika igubha usuku lwentsha .
NgoJuni 16 kusuke kukhunjulwa ukuzidela kwabafundi baseSoweto , ababezabalaza nokwaholela ekutheni abanye abafundi babulawe ngamaphoyisa , ngesikhathi bebhikishela isiphakamiso sokuthi kufundwe ngolimi lwesiBhunu .
Izinselelo ezibhekene nentsha yanamhlanje azifani nalezo zango - 1976 .
Ngeshwa nentsha yamanje isabhekana nokucwaswa ngokwebala njengoba sibonile kugonyuluka abafundi abafunda ezikoleni zabelungu lapho abafundi babantu abamnyama besuke beyingcosana khona .
Kuyadabukisa ukuthi ngo - 2020 kusaliwa impi yebala kodwa le mpi isazoqhubeka uma kusazothi kukhulunywa ngayo kujahwe ukumbambatha , kube ngabacwasi abashaya imithetho yokuthi kumele siyikhulume kanjani le ndaba futhi kube khona abathi abantu abamnyama bayathanda ukukhala ngokucwaswa isidingo singekho .
Ngaphezu kokucwaswa ngokwebala inselelo enkulu intsha yanamhlanje ebhekene nayo ukuntuleka kwemisebenzi .
Miningi imizamo ekhona yokulwa nalokhu kushoda kwemisebenzi kodwa ziningi ezinye izinto eziyimixhantela yakho ezidinga ukulungiswa ukuze imizamo izothela izithelo .
Eminye yale mixhantela ububha , ukungalingani kwemfundo etholwa yintsha yaseNingizimu Afrika , ukungafinyeleli kwamathuba kuyona yonke intsha , ukungabi bikho kwengqalasizinda kwezinye izingxenye zezwe , ukungabi nolwazi ngokushintsha kwezinto nomthelela wezobuchwepheshe , ingcindezi intsha ebhekene nayo nezinye izimo zempilo .
Kuyadingeka ukuthi uma kukhulunywa ngokusiza intsha kubhekwe yonke into hhayi uhlangothi ololudwa kuphela .
Kumqoka nokuthi kukhunjulwe ukuthi abantu abathandi izinto ezifanayo ngakho akungathi uma kubekwa etafuleni iziphakamiso ngezinto ezingasiza intsha kwenziwe lokho ngendlela eyodwa noma kucatshangwe ukuthi wonke umuntu kumele lokhu okuphakanyiswayo kumsebenzele .
Akuyona yonke intsha efuna ukuzisebenza , akuyona yonke efuna ukusebenza ngezobuchwepheshe futhi akuyona yonke ezosebenza kwezikaqedisizungu .
Asiyeseke intsha ngendlela ezosiza yona futhi asizwe kuyona ukuthi iyiphi indlela edinga ukusizwa ngayo .
Asixazulule izinkinga , siyeke ukulwa sodwa singama - Afrika
MHLELI : Ngithanda ukuzwakalisa uvo lwami .
Mayelana nendaba ephume kwiSolezwe ngomhlaka - 6 Septhemba .
Isihloko besithi : Kuvalwa izitolo zabokufika ngenxa yokwesaba .
Bengifuna ukuveza ukukhathazeka nokudumala ngesenzo esenziwa ngabahlali bakuleli becwasa abokufika .
Akusibona bonke abakufika abafika nobudlwangudlwangu kuleli likaMthayina .
Abanye bafike ngokuzothola impilo engcono abazosimamisa ngayo imindeni yabo esele emazweni abo .
Kungasibona futhi bonke abahleli ngokungemthetho lapha ezweni lethu .
Impela ngizalwe emuva kwenkululeko yaseNingizimu Afrika .
Kepha umlando esengike ngawuzwa ukuthi amaqabane naboMkhonto Wesizwe babefuna indawo yokufihla ikhanda kuwona la mazwe ngenkathi izwe lethu lisabhekene nobunzima bobandlululo .
Kungani manje sizobulalana sodwa , sixhaphaze impahla yabo njengoba kwenzekile Kwandonga ziyaduma .
Sekuchaphazeleke nakuleli likaBhanana njengoba eTshelimnyama sekubalwa izigameko ezinjenga lezi .
Kungabe sisadiniwe ukuthi bahleli kule lizwe noma sesiyabantshontshela okungokwabo , abafike bazakhela kona mabefika kuleli ?
Kuyadumaza okwenzeke kuleya ndawo nakwezinye ezichaphazelwe ilolu dweshu lokulwisana nabokufika .
Liveza isithombe esibi ngabantu bakuleli .
Ngiyazwelana nokuthi abahlali bakuleli bazizwa sengathi uhulumeni akabanakile kodwa unakekela abantu bangaphandle .
Besingatholwa isixazululo ngaphandle kokuzwisa omunye umuntu ubuhlungu .
IsiZulu sithi okoniwe ngomlomo kulungiswa ngomlomo .
Asibumbaneni silungise izinkinga zethu njengendlu emnyama .
Singazibukisi nabezizwe sibulalana sodwa , sigcwele inzondo yokucwasa odadewethu nabafowethu .

Masifunde ukonga imali nokugwema izikweletu
NGIYATHEMBA ningene kahle onyakeni omusha .
Konje nithe uyanicika lo mbuzo ?
Pho sizokwenzanjani ngoba sesijwayele ukubuzana phela ukuthi singene kanjani ? Sethemba ukuthi imali isekhona emabhange akekho ozosibelesela ngeklabishi nophuthu , ngoba imali siyisebenzisa kahle .
Ngiyacela njengoba kuqala unyaka sihlele kahle imali yethu , ukuze sazi izidingo ezinqala , izinto ezingenasidingo esichitha kuzo imali , siphinde songe .
Kubuhlungu ukubona abantu beme kolayini abade ababheke komashonisa beyoboleka imali yokuya emsebenzini neyokuthenga umfaniswano wesikole sezingane .
Ngangicelile ngoDisemba ukuthi , anothi uma senithenga inyama , iziphuzo negilosa bese nithenga nomfaniswano wesikole .
Kulo nyaka ngicela sizwane nabangani esizodlala nabo izitokofela zokulondoloza imali .
Ngisho noma ungaqala ngokubeka uR100 ngenyanga , leyo mali iyawenza umehluko .
Imali ayibekwa ngumuntu osebenzayo kuphela kodwa nabahola imali yesibonelelo kahulumeni bangabeka noma uR20 ngenyanga , ozokwazi ukubalekelela ezidingweni zabo .
Ngiphatheka kabi uma ngibona odadewethu begcwele ezinxanxatheleni zezitolo uma kuphela inyanga , sekungene imali .
Ngiye ngizibuze ukuthi ngabe babeka malini nokuthi baphoqelekile yini ukuyokhithiza ngosuku lokuqala enyangeni .
Kulo nyaka ngiyacela ukuthi sonke sifunde ukulondoloza imali , lokho okuncane esikutholayo kufanele sikucaze kahle kube khona imali esiphila ngayo nemali esiyilondolozayo .
Siyazi ukuthi umnotho wezwe awukhuli kahle ngakho kudingeka ukuthi sonke sizame ukuwuhlelela ngokucophelela .
Uma ningenaso isiqiniseko sokuthi inkampani enitshala kuyo imali isemthethweni noma cha ngicela nithinte iFinancial Sector Conduct Authority ( FSCA ) okuyiyona elawula izinkampani ezisebenza ngemali eNingizimu Afrika . I - FSCA itholakala ku - 800 110 443 noma ngokuvakashela iwebsite yayo ethi www . fsca . co . za .
* Ngithintwe ngumthengi obefuna ukuthenga igolide kwenye inkampani manje efuna ukwazi ukuthi ngabe isemthethweni yini .
- Uma inkampani ithi idayisa igolide noma okunye okumbiwa phansi ngiyacela nithinte iFSCA nibone ukuthi leyo nkampani ivunyelwe yini ukudayisa leyo mpahla ethi iyayidayisa nokuthi umsebenzi ewenzayo usemthethweni yini .
- Mina ngazi ukuthi igolide limbiwa ezimayini kodwa zikhona nezinkampani okuthiwa zinegunya lokulidayisa kuhle ukwenza isiqiniseko sokuthi zivumelekile ukwenza lo msebenzi ngaphambi kokutshala imali yakho kuzona .
* NgoDisemba bengifonelwa ngabantu bekhala ngezitolo ezibadayisela ukudla okubolile nefenisha engekho sesimeni esifanele .
- Uma udayiselwe ukudla okubolile kubalulekile ukuthi uqale ufake isikhalo kuleso sitolo esikudayisele ukudla okubolile .
Uthinte nehhovisi labathengi baso ngaphambi kokuthi ungishayele ucingo .
Mina ngingenelela uma kuwukuthi abakusizi ngalutho .
- Uma uthenge ifenisha engekho esimeni esikahle nakhona kufanele uqale ufake isikhalo esitolo .
Uma bengakusizi , usungaxhumana nami . - Ungayithinta iConsumer Goods and Services Ombudsman ( CGSO ) etholakala ku - 860 272 noma ku - www . cgso . org . za * Uma unenkinga edinga usizo lwezabathengi ungathumela i - email [ email protected ]
Ziningi izindawo ezidinga ukuhlanjululwa ngokwesintu
Lihle iqiniso , asingalokhu siya le nalena , ngabe sithi liyafa izwe ?
Sesifike esikhathini lapho kufanele singama - Afrika sizibuze ukuthi inkululeko esasiyilwela ngakube eyokuhlala nokuthenga imizi yabelungu , ukuba sezikhundleni ababeziphethe noma kwabe kungukukhululeka kwemimoya yamathongo ase - Afrika , namagugu akhona njengalokhu saphucwa sakhohliswa ngakho ?
Ngakube kwakungukubuyela emuva ezindleleni esasenza ngazo esathelwa ngobhici sangabe sisazibona ?
Kuningi esingakubuza kulokhu esikubiza ngenkululeko .
Sithi izingane zethu zifunda ezikoleni zabamhlophe , zikhuluma isingisi , olwazo ulimi ziyalwesaba , luyasehlisa , sifunda amaphephandaba ezinye izilimi awethu do .
Le mibuzo ngiyibuza ngoba izwe lithathwe labekwa ezandleni zomuntu omnyama okunguyena owalahlekelwa kodwa uma ubheka konakala ezandleni zakhe futhi nguyena okhuthaza ukonakala okwenzekayo .
Ngokwesintu sase - Afrika kwakuthi uma kuvele isehlakalo endaweni noma inxiwa lelo lingcolisekile , lalihlanjululwa .
Uma abababili kade bengabonanga ngaso linye kwakhona umsindo nokuxabana kwenziwe usiko lokuthelelana amanzi ukuze nezidalwa ezilele zibuyise izibusiso ezase zilahlekile .
Ngikusho lokhu ngoba izwe liya ngokuya lishona phansi ngenxa yomlando ongazange walungiseka sesithe sikhululekile .
Ngesonto eledlule singakayi kude , bukela insambatheka eyenzeke ePhalamende .
Kuthiwa uwayengumengameli ngesikhathi sobandlululo , uMnu FW de Klerk , akaphume ePhalamende .
Lowo ongumengameli wamabhizinisi kahulumeni naye akaxoshwe .
Umbuzo engisale nawo emuva kwakho konke okwenzekile , ngakube bayimbangela yini yokuthi izwe nomnotho walo kube la kukhona namhlanje ?
Impendulo ithi cha .
Ucha wami umi ekutheni sathatha izintambo zikahulumeni kunezindawo eziningi ezazingcolisekile namhlanje eseziyinkinga .
Umnuz Pravin Gordhan njengamanje nguyena owengemele wonke amabhinisi kahulumeni .
Izinkinga zala mabhizinisi zisuka la : inkampani yezindiza , i - SAA yayithwala izikhali zokuyobulala okwakuthiwa amaphekulazikhuni , aphinde agibelise bona ababeyothatha izinqumo zokubulala ababelwelwa inkululeko .
IDenel yakha izikhali zokubulala amaphekulazikhuni , inhlangano yokusakaza iSABC yayisetshenziselwa ukuhlwanyela amanga ngokwenzekile , kwabe kungumshini wamanga wamabhunu .
I - Eskom kwabe kuyingodla kagesi owawukhanyisela bona kuphela , iTransnet eyingxenye ngezinqola zokuthutha esasingakwazi , nazo izikhali . Umbuzo uthi zonke lezi zikhungo zahlanjululwa yini ?
Ngesikhathi uhulumeni usudlulela kwabamnyama kwakukhona konke lokhu kungcola .
Nabo abamnyama qobo bahlenzekile yini izandla zabo ngokwemindeni yabo ? Kuningi okwenzeka ePhalamende .
Umengameli owuphahla nensika yobandlululo , uVerwoerd , wabulawelwa khona ePhalamende .
Lagezwa sathathwa isithunzi sakhe ?
Imithetho eminingi yobandlululo beyishayelwa kulo .
Uma sekungena thina abamnyama kunhlanjuliliwe lokho ? Ibhilidi likahulumeni , i - Union Building namhlanje okumiswe isithombe sikaMandela emagcekeni alo , lihlanjululiwe ?
Ave isithombe sikaMandela simiswe phezu kokungcola kwangaleso sikhathi ? Bukela okwenzeka emanyuvesi .
Sijabule sagxuma sabheka phezulu kuthiwa emanyuvesi sekuzofundwa ndawonye .
Ayephethe izifundiswa ezimhlophe ezazingafuni lutho .
Uyakhumbula eWits usolwazi omhlophe owaziwisa ebhilidini wancamela ukuzibulala inyuvesi izophathwa ngomnyama ?
E - DUT namhlanje kufa abafundi belekanyana , akukho lutho olwenziwayo kwenzenjani ?
Ngabe ngumlando noma ngabaphathiswe lenyuvesi ?
Zikhona izimpendulo zakho konke lokhu .
Ngiyishiya kuwena umfundo uyetshise . Bhedlindaba
Akuqiniswe ezokuphepha emanyuvesi
MHLELI : Ake ngiphawule ngalolu daba lokungaqini kwezokuphepha ezikoleni ngoba maningi amacala asebikiwe mayelana nezitshudeni ezishonela emagcekeni esikole okuyinto engayinhle ngoba abazali basuke bethembe ukuthi izingane zabo zivikelekile .
Siyizitshudeni sibhekene nezinkinga eziningi sizizwa singaphephile emanyuvesi .
Sekukaningi sizwa kuthiwa isitshudeni silimale singaphakathi enyuvesi .
Kushone isitshudeni eDUT ngenxa yodlame nokungabibikho kwezokuphepha eziqinile futhi akukho okwenzekayo noma izinyathelo azithathiwe ukukhombisa ukuthi bazoboshwa ababulele isitshudeni .
Kungasijabulisa ukuthi abasezikhundleni kuhulumeni bangenele kulolu daba ngoba kubonakala sengathi bayahluleka abaphathi benyuvesi .
Okubuhlungu wukuthi konke lokhu okwenzekile kwenzeke emakilasini okufunda .
Sesiyesaba nokuyofunda ngoba sizizwa singavikelekile futhi nabazali bethu bathukile ngalesi sigameko .
Kunzima uma sekwenzeka izinto ezifana nalezi .
Emanyuvesi nasezikoleni kumele kunyuswe izinga lezokuphepha ukuze izitshudeni zivikeleke nokufunda kuqhubeke kahle .
Limuncu leli hlaya lamaphoyisa kamasipala
MHLELI : Kwelakho eliwela umfula ugcwele , ngithi ake ngizwakalise ilaka lami .
Le nto ngizoyibiza ngokumosha izinsizakusebenza , ukumosha uphethroli , imali yomkhandlu kanti ngaphezu kwakho konke iyihlaya elingahlekisi .
Mhlawumbe yimi nomphakathi esingayazi inhloso yalokhu okwenzekayo .
Ake ngiqale ngoMlaza laphaya emarobhothini eMega City .
Esikhathini esiningi laphaya eMega City ufica imoto yamaphoyisa omkhandlu ikhanyisa amalambu aluhlaza .
Uma ubheka phakathi , ubone iphoyisa noma amaphoyisa ezidlalela ngamafoni , lapho i - traffic emarobhothini idla lubi .
Amatekisi azingenela noma ikanjani nje lawa aphuma edolobheni , izimoto eziphuma eMega city ngaphakathi zishaye ujenga kungahambeki .
Umbuzo wami uthi ameleni laphaya njengoba ezihlalele ngaphakathi ezimotweni esikhundleni sokuthi ahlele ukuhamba kwezimoto kwisiminyaminya ?
Kunaloko uzowathola emisa izimoto ezihlola , ukuthi kwenzakalani emarobhothini , kawanamsebenzi .
Okufanayo nokewenzeka kwaV emarobhothini .
Sicela umphathi wamaphoyisa asicacisele ngokwenzeka laphaya ukuze sazi , singabi nemibuzo .
Inceku ihlulwe wumona ngoBeekay
MHLELI : Kwelakho eliyaye likhombise ukungachemi nelifundwa ngabantu abaningi ngenxa yolimi olunothile , ngiyacela ukuba ungiphe isikhandlana ngikhulise uzakwethu uMbhishobhi Themba Chonco ngakubhalile kwelakho lapho ethe khona " Alubhekisiswe uhlelo lukaBeekay . " "
Kuyiqiniso ukuthi inkomo iyalushayelwa ubisi lwayo .
Emva kokufunda udaba olubhalwe nguGambushe nokuwumbono wakhe , yebo kuleli lizwe sinelungelo lokubeka imibono yethu kodwa ayingadumazi - ke abanye .
Uyabona lo mbono kaGambushe uyangidumaza ngoba uphuma kwinceku ezwakala ihlulwa wumona yaze yawukhiphela ngaphandle .
Mhlawumbe Gambushe kuzofanele wazi ukuthi uhlelo lukaBeekay Mchunu ( osesithombeni ) akazisuseli yena ekhanda kepha usuke enikwe indlela ewumhlahlandlela eyinikwa umphathizinhlelo .
Uyabona umphathizinhlelo wayizama le ndlela yokufaka uDr Mahaye ekutheni asibuyisele esintwini nebala kwenzeka ngempela njengoba abalaleli balwamukela ngesasasa uhlelo lukaMchunu .
Okunye okumele ukwazi Gambushe wukuthi lolu hlelo luwuhlelo olulalelwa kakhulu ekubeni lungena ngeSabatha kanye nje vo futhi lulele isithathu ezinhlelweni zoKhozi FM ngokulalelwa .
Angithandi ingane yomuntu siyidlele umona nceku ngemisebenzi yayo emihle , empeleni njengoba mina nawe sizinceku simelwe ukuhalalisa imisebenzi emihle eyenziwayo .
Angifuni ukuthi uMchunu asizwe kabi singabalaleli bakhe ngoba izinkomba zithi mina nawe siyamlalela okusho ukuthi uyasinika lokhu esikudingayo .
Kumele engabe abalandeli bamaNazaretha bayakhala ngokuthi banikwa usuku olulodwa okuyaye kube yiSabatha ekubeni ezinye izinkolo zinikwa inkonzo yangesonto , kunokuba bakhale bayamemana .
Sengiphetha uboke uvakashe eBuhleni uyolunguza ukuthi amasiko esintu kawekho yini kuleli bandla .
Uma uphika Gambushe uthi iNazareth Baptist Church akusilo isonto eliphethe isintu , lilethe lelo phambili ukuze uBeekay alicubungule .
ILotto ngeke isathenjwa
MHLELI : Ake ngiveze umbono wami ngophenyo lweSpecial Investigation Unit ( SIU ) , ngokusebenza nokwenzeka kwiLotto .
Njengoba iSIU imatasa iqoqa ulwazi lwamakhompyutha nemiqingo kwiLotto , ngineqiniso lokhuthi uphenyo balwenza ngoba bazi ukuthi vele amantshontso kade kwase edliwa .
Lokhu kufumbathisana kuthiwa bekwenziwa ngamalungu asezikhundleni eziphezulu egixabeza abangani nezihlobo zawo imali .
Ngicabanga ukuthi yinto ekhona leyo sekuyikho nje ukuqoqa ubufakazi bese ziyochithana enkantolo .
Njengoba uphenyo luzogxila eminyakeni ewu - 6 eyedlule , ngibona lokhu kuzokwenza iLotto ingathenjwa kakhulu kunakuqala .
Kodwa Ithuba , elengamele iLotto lapha eNingizimu Afrika , lizongathenjwa ukusebenza kwalo .
Ngikusho lokhu ngoba Ithuba alikaqedi ngisho iminyaka ewu - 10 lisebenzisana nabakwaLotto .
Yingakho abantu bezoyingabaza iLotto neThuba .
Phela kuthiwa kayinuki ingosiwe .
Sesobabona bevela enkantolo abayosile , cishe abanye kade bengakayidli , abanye sebeyidlile ngalokho - ke bayobe badle icala benobhululu babo .
Kade besikelana amantshontso benqakisana nangamathenda , kungalandelwa indlela eqondile yokuwakhipha kwawo .
Sengathi kungavela konke okuyiqiniso ngalezi zinsolo .
Okubi nje wukuthi isithunzi nokwethenjwa kweLotto kuzokwehla kubantu .
Kuyangijabulisa nokho ukuthi abakwaLotto bahlezi bebuyisela emphakathini .
Phela kuvamile ukuba baxhase izinhlangano ezingayenzi inzuzo .
Nezikole banakho ukuzixhasa ngokulungisa ingqalasizinda yokudlala nangemifaniswano yokudlala .
Bayaxhasa nangezinto ezifana nemitapo yolwazi enobucwepheshe besimanje , okuyinto ebaluleke kakhulu leyo ukunciphisa umthwalo emahlombe kahulumeni .
Likhulu kakhulu iqhaza elidlalwa yiLotto emphakathini .
Kodwa iqiniso kwabanukwayo kumele livele futhi lizovela .
Ngiyayithanda nendlela iSIU , amaHawks nophiko lwezokushushisa abaphapheme ngayo kule minyaka embalwa edlule .
Phela lezi zinhlaka kade sezifana nenja engenamazinyo . Sibahle NgobeseENQUTHU
UNgizwenkosi uyaziphoxa ngokukhulumela futhi
MHLELI : Ngisacela unginike isikhadlana ngizwakalise ilaka lami ngomsakazi ebengimkhonzile uNgizwenkosi Mlandowamachunu Mchunu ( osesithombeni ) .
Yize esengekho kwezokusakaza kodwa uyohlale engumsakazi engimkhonzile .
Ukumkhonza kwami yingoba ubesiqhakambisa isiZulu emsakazweni Ukhozi FM nokuyinto esilahlekile manje ngenxa yokuthi iningi labasakazi lizibona lilahla uma lisakaza ngesizulu .
Ngizoke ngingene ngithi ntshi ekungezwaneni kwakhe nowayenguzakwabo uTshathugodo Khathide Ngobe .
Ngithi wayenguzakwabo nje yingoba babehubha uhlelo uSigiya Ngengoma nanokusebenza ndawonye emsakazweni Ukhozi , yize sewakhonjwa indlela ekubeni uTshatha yena esayibambile .
Ingxabano ebukeka isusa uNgizwe isiyasinenga thina bantu bakuleli .
Okwenza sinengeke ngukuthi uMacingwane uneconsi nochuku okuyinto engafuneki kubantu ubona singayindawo nje .
Uchuku lususwe uNgizwe walusabalalisa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana .
Sengiyifundile yonke into ake ayisho ngoTshatha okubukeka emsukela ngoba zolo lokhu bebengamathe nolimi besasakazela Ukhozi .
Mina bengingalindele ukuthi uNgizwe uzokhulumisa okomuntu ongawubonanga umbombo kathisha .
Ukukhuluma kwakhe kabi ngoTshatha sikuthathe njengomuntu ovimba ngempumelelo yomunye umntwana .
Phela singabalaleli siyazi ukuthi bebengamathe nolimi futhi ubungeke ubahlukanise nhlobo kodwa kumanje sesizwa izindaba .
Okungenze ngaloba kwelakho ukuthi usabise imbongi engiyibiza ngembongi yamaqiniso uKwazi Nsele .
Umfoka Nsele usezakhele udumo ngokusho into eyiqiniso njengoba ebuze ngamathuna aseGoli nje kodwa uNgizwe usemsabise ngokuthi umfana uncome uTshatha ngokushayela uSigiya Ngengoma kahle .
Mina ngisasho nje ukuthi uNgizwe akehlise umoya bese ebhekana nenselelo akuyo ayeke phansi ingane enhle njengonina uThembi yenze into esegazini kuyo okuwukusakaza .
UKhongolose uchizela abavoti bakhe
Mhleli : Kwelakho eliwela umfula ugcwele , ngenhlonipho ngiyacela ukudlulisa ilaka lami ngempatho esiyitshengiswa yiqembu elibusayo .
Kuyacaca manje ukuthi ukungasebenzi kwentsha ezweni uhulumeni ukwenza ihlaya .
UMengameli wezwe uthembise abantu izijumbana zokudla ukuze bathibe indlala , waphinde wabathembisa umhlomulo kaR350 engikhuluma nje kukhona abangakazitholi izimpendulo ngezicelo zabo , bebe bathenjiswa .
Kuyadabukisa ukubona iqembu elibusayo lichizela abavoti balo ngalolu hlobo .
Yayiqinisile ingwevu kwezokuhlaziya ipolitiki , uSolwazi Somadoda Fikeni , uma ithi abanye abantu bavotela igama leqembu kanti abanye bavotela izenzo zalo .

Asithobele umyalelo kamengameli wokuvala izwe
MHLELI : Okokuqala mangizwakalise ukubonga kuwo wonke amakholwa ngokuhlonipha kwawo abambisane nohulumeni ekumiseni ukuhlanganyela futhi abekezele ahloniphe ngoba ecabangela impilo yezakhamuzi zaseNingizimu Afrika nabo bonke abakuleli zwe .
Ngizibonga izinkolo ngokwehlukana kwazo okubandakanya amaKhrestu , amaNazaretha , amaSulumane , amaHindu , abenkolo yesintu nezinye ekumiseni imikhuleko eba ndawonye besabele kwikhwelo likaMengameli Cyril Ramaphosa neziphathimandla zonke zaseNingizimu Afrika .
Singekhohlwe uNgangezwelakhe noNdunankulu kaZulu , uMntwana waKwaPhindangene , amakhosi asendlunkulu wonkana ngomlomo womntwana izinyane lesilo ( umntwana uNhlanganiso ) alidlulisele ezinduneni zonke lapha eGoli .
Izwi lafinyelela emphakathini lokuthobela isibalo sokuhlangana kwabayikhulu ndawonye sasheshe safika kithina nokuthi siqhubeke ngemfundiso endala yenhlanzeko yananelwa yisizwe ikakhulukazi lapha eGauteng .
Yingakho nalokhu kokuvalwa kusheshe kwezwakala kwahlonishwa ngoba nezinduna bezilishumayela lelo vangeli .
Yebo yize izingqinamba zibe khona futhi zisekhona , ikakhulukazi kwezamabhizinisi okubandakanya nemboni yamatekisi kodwa ukuthobela umthetho kumele sikubonge .
Babenezingxoxo nohulumeni ezinokuthula nokuvikela isizwe .
Ngicela ukubonga bonke abaholi bamaqembu aphikisayo ngokukhuluma ngezwi elilodwa .
Ngicela ukuba nombono wokuthi ongqongqoshe abamele i - NCCC ( National Coronavirus Command Council ) bangazishiyi ngaphandle izinhlaka ezithintekayo ezinqumeni abazithathayo .
Kuhle baxhumane nezinhlaka ezithintekayo ngaphambi kokuba bayomemezela okanye benze isithangami sabezindaba esishiya thina mphakathi sinemibuzo engaphenduleki .
Yiqiniso sinamaqembu ethu ezombusazwe ngokwehlukana kodwa uma niwashiya kude sizobuza kuwo singatholi zimpendulo ezigculisayo .
Makubanjiswane . Ngicela umnyango wezempilo ulibuyekeze kabusha uhlaka oluzongena emakhaya luzosihlolela iCoronavirus .
Sinemibuzo yokuthi ngabe umnyango wezempilo ikakhulu lapha eGauteng ubathathephi labo abazosebenza , ubaqashe nini wabaqeqesha nini ?
Futhi usebenzise ziphi izindlela ukubaqasha ?

Anoqaphela izicagogwana zamaqembu okhethweni
Uma kusondela izinketho , ziningi izigigaba ezivelayo ezinye zazo wukukhandwa kwamaqembu amasha isigubhukane ukuze nabasunguli awo bacoshacoshe emavotini ukuze badle bacwebezele izisu .
Nokho - ke angikho lapho .
Njengelungu lokuqina leNFP , ngithi angikhuze bonke laba abakhanda izipaza zamaqenjana abo ukuthi abahlukane nokuthi uma bekhuluma nabezindaba bathi bavela kuNFP .
Ngizobhekisa kakhulu eqenjini le - ABC naleli elethulwe ngesonto eledlule elibizwa nge - Apemo .
Ngiyabaxwayisa ukuthi abadlale ibhola bangadlali indoda .
Le politiki yabo ayisasebenzi , abangafundi ukuma ngeNFP .
Amaqembu abo awekho ezingeni leNFP .

I - ABC ne - Apemo kabekho ndawo , siyoqala ukubabiza ngamaqembu ezepolitiki angempela uma sebemelelekile ngokwezihlalo ePhalamende .
Okwamanje sisengasho ukuthi basengamaqhumamponjwana amaqembu .

I - Eff ifike kwezwakala yadlondlobala
I - EFF kulo nyaka ibigubha iminyaka eyisikhombisa selokhu yasungulwa ngo - 2013 kodwa uma singabheka amagalelo esiwakhombisile , ungathi yinhlangano ekade yaba khona .
Uma sibheka ukudlondlobala kwayo , kubonakale ngokuthi ikhuphule isibalo sayo samalungu ayimele eziShayamthetho nasePhalamende eCape Town .
Ngo - 2014 , okwakuwunyaka wokhetho lukazwelonke nolwezifundazwe , KwaZulu - Natal yahlomula ngezihlalo ezimbili kuphela , kwathi kuzwelonke yaba neziwu - 25 .
Ngonyaka odlule KwaZulu - Natal ivuke nezihlalo eziyisishiyagalombili , kwathi kuzwelonke yathola eziwu - 44 .
Lapha kubalwa nesibalo samakhansela elibe nawo ngo - 2016 , abalelwa ngaphezu kuka - 800 ezweni lonke , KwaZulu - Natal bathola awu - 64 .
Lokho kukhomba ukuthi abantu baseNingizimu Afrika bayakholelwa kuyo .
IsiZulu sithi ingwe idla ngamabala .
Lokhu kufakazelwa yindlela edlondlobala ngayo ngokwezibalo .
Lokhu kuwubufakazi bokuthi isenza lokhu abantu abakudingayo nokubathokozisayo .
Ngesikhathi isungulwa , abahlaziyi nabaphrofethi bamanga abayinikanga thuba , bathi izoshabalala kuhle kwamazolo ebona ilanga .
Baze bayifanisa nezinye izinhlangano ezasungulwa ngaphambi kwayo .
Ikhombisile kodwa ukuthi ize kule ndima yazi kahle ukuthi abantu baseNingizimu Afrika badingani .
Ukufika kwe - EFF kwenze abantu abansundu babuyelwa yithemba ngoba iyabalwela ezimeni okubalwa kuzo ukuhlukunyezwa emsebenzini nasekucwasweni ngokwebala .
Sekube nezinto eziningi esezenzekile okubalwa kuzo isitolo esakhangisa izimpahla zokugqoka i - H & M eyayilulaza isithunzi somuntu omnyama .
Ukungenelela kwe - EFF kwenza lesi setolo sehlela ngezansi saxolisa ezweni ngesenzo saso .
Muva nje isitolo iClicks sikhiphe isikhangiso esasibukela phansi isithunzi somuntu omnyama .
Lokho kubange ukuthi kube khona imibhikisho , lesi sitolo savalwa izwe lonke .
Konke lokhu i - EFF ikwenza ngokulwela ibala lomuntu omnyama , ingakhathalele ukuthi ungowaliphi iqembu lezepolitiki .
Yiso lesi sizathu esenza ukuthi ngithi ingene kulo mdlalo wepolitiki seyazi ukuthi izokwenzani futhi konke ekwenzayo ikwenza ngempumelelo .
Umbuzo ongaqhamuka ngothi izenzo zayo zibenzelani abantu baseNingizimu Afrika ? Ngabe sizobona le nhlangano idlondlobala isuka ekubeni yiqembu lesithathu elikhulu ekulawulweni kwezwe iba ngelesibili noma ngelokuqala na ? Uma kodwa ubheka lapho isuka khona nesikhathi esikusona njengamanje , kuyabonakala ukuthi isithunzi somuntu omnyama sibonakala
sivikeleka kakhulu , nabantu bebuyelwa yithemba .
Sengiphetha nje , ngithi ngabe kuzokwenzekani okhethweni lohulumeni basekhaya okulindeleke ukuthi lube ngonyaka ozayo ? Ngabe ekwenzile i - EFF phambilini kuzoyizuzisa amavoti amaningi ? Konke sekulele kubavoti ukuthi ngabe bafuna ivoti labo libenzeleni .
Kubalulekile ukuphepha ezikoleni
KUPHELILE ukuphola .
Ziyavulwa izikole ngoJuni 1 .
Ingabe sikulungele yini lokhu ? Lona ngumbuzo osezingqondweni zabazali nabafundi bakaGrade 7 no - 12 njengoba kuyibo abazoqala babuyele esikoleni uma kuqala inyanga ezayo ngokwesimemezelo soMnyango weMfundo eyisiSekelo .
Noma ziziningi izingqinamba ezibhekene noMnyango wezeMfundo kuleli kepha ngiyakuncoma ukukhombisa ukuhleleka kwalo mnyango ngandlela thile .
Noma isekhona imibuzo ngezinhlelo zokuqikelela ukuvikeleka kwabantwana kodwa ukuqala ngedlanzana ngaphambi kokubuyisela bonke abantwana emagunjini okufunda kukhombisa khona ukuthi icatshangiwe le ndaba .
Kusekhona - ke esisazibuza khona ukuthi ngabe kuhleliwe yini ngaphambi kokuvulwa kwezikole .
Kulokhu singabala ukuhlanzisisa ukuze kubulawe amagciwane athwele isifo iCovid - 19 .
Kuzofanele kube nezibulalimagciwane nokunye okubulala amagciwane , kulungiswe nesimo samanzi ukuze abantwana bahlanze izandla njengoba imigomo yokuvikela lolu bhubhane isho .
Ngokwemibiko ye - United Nations Educational , Scientific and Cultural Organisation ( Unesco ) okukhona ngaphansi kwayo iNigizimu Afrika , India , USA , China , Mexico , France , Turkey , Brazil , Australia , Egypt , Greece , United Kingdom , Canada , Saudi Arabia , New Zealand , Norway , Denmark , Lebanon namanye amazwe ; zilinganiselwa ku - 90 % izikole ezivaliwe emazweni angu - 186 ngenxa yegciwane iCorona emhlabeni jikelele .
UTUMELO Moloi efutha i - hydrogen peroxide eyisibulalimagciwane .
Yena nozakwabo uBheki Rachilo noDada Maseko bagqugquzela ukuthi kufuthwe ezikoleni ukuze kuphephe abantwanaZikhona izikole emazweni ambalwa lapho abantwana sebeqalile ukubuyela esikoleni okuzofanela sibukele kuwo ukuze sinqande ukubhebhetheka kwalesi sifo ukuze nempilo ibuyele kweyejwayelekile kancane kancane .
Lapha singabala amazwe afana neChina , Japan neDenmark .
La mazwe ashintshe izinhlelo zawo zokuhlanzwa nokuphathwa kwezikole ukuze kuphephe abantwana .
Izikole zifuthiwe , zahlanzwa ngaphambi kokuthi abantwana baqale ukufunda .
Nathi eNingizimu Afrika kasiqhelelene nokwenza uhlobo olunzulu nolukhethekile lokuhlanza nokubulala amagciwane ezikoleni nasemahhovisi .
UTumelo Moloi nozakwabo uDada Maseko noBheki Rachilo beMist Hygiene , eThekwini naseGoli , babone ukubaluleka kwalo msebenzi bahlanganisa amakhanda bakwenza kwenzeka .
" Siqala ngokuhlola ibhilidi , bese sisebenzisa imishini yethu ekhipha okusantuthu okumhlophe okuthwele i - hydrogen peroxide okuyiyona ebulala kwasani eyigciwane elingaba khona endaweni , " kuchaza uTumelo .
Uthe abantu bavumeleka ukungena kuleso sakhiwo emva kwehora uma umsebenzi wokuhlanza sewenziwe .
Uthe uma sekufuthiwe , kubalulekile ukufaka imishini yokufutha abantu ngaphambi kokuthi bangene kuleso sakhiwo esesishlanziwe .
Nesibulalimagciwane siyadingeka ukuze abantu noma abantwana bahlanze izandla okuyizo ezisabalalisa amagciwane ngokuthintathinta .
Kuzobaluleka ukusebenzisana kwabaphathi bezemfundo nongqondongqondo bokuhlanza izakhiwo ikakhulukazi ezikoleni lapho abantwana bethu befunda khona .
Uma kungabanjiswana , ukubhebhetheka kweCovid - 19 singakunqanda ezikoleni ukuze imfundo iqhubeke .
Lokhu singekwenze ngokuhlanza nje kuphela kepha nokuqikelela ukuthi : Abantwana bethu bagqoka izifonyo ngaso sonke isikhathi .
Abafundi nothisha abagulayo bahlale futhi banakekelwe emakhaya .
Baqikekelele ukungathintathintani kwabafundi nothisha .
Sibakhumbuze ukugeza izandla ngaso sonke isikhathi ngensipho noma ngesibulalimagciwane kahlanu noma ngaphezulu ngosuku .
Ukushiya isikhala phakathi kwabo .
Ukungahlangani kwabafundi abaningi ndawonye , okusho ukuthi imidlalo yokuzilolonga ithi ukumiswa ezikoleni .
Ukuqikelela ukuthi abafundi banikezwa ulwazi olubafanele nabazoluqonda nge - Covid - 19 .

Luyancomeka ushintsho emsakazweni Ukhozi FM
MHLELI : Ngiyakhuleka kunina beSilo , nina beNkashana kaMenzi eyaphuza umlaza ngameva .
Ngiyathokoza ukuthola ithuba lokubhala kulo iphephandaba Isolezwe eliwela umfula ugcwele , yimi induna yamaBhinca kuzwe lonke Sizwe Ndlovu , Kwasjula .

Ngithi kuye uwushayile umsebenzi wakhe kwezinye zezinhlelo , ngizoqala ngohlelo lwasekuseni Vuka Afrika .
Lolu hlelo lumnandi ngendlela eyisimanga , uyezwa ukuthi abasakazi bayinto ehlangene futhi bakwenza ukhohlwe yizinsizi zakho ekuseni uye emsebenzini ngomfutho .
Ngithanda indlela uSipho Mbatha enza ngayo uyakhombisa ukuthi uvuthiwe kulento yokusakaza .

Ugologo nelanga akuyibulali iCorona
ZININGI izigigaba emlandweni womhlaba ezisikhombisa ukuthi izikhathi ezinzima njengalesi esizithola sikuso kuyenzeka ziveze ngokusobala isibindi nomoya wobumbano ezweni .
Kusukela ngesikhathi kumenyezelwa okokuqala ukufika kweCorona kwelakithi ngoMashi 5 nonyaka , ngihlabeke umxhwele ngomkhombandlela nokwesekeka esikuthola ebuholi bethu , kusukela kuMengameli Cyril Ramaphosa , kuye kuNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo uDkt Zweli Mkhize ,
kuze kufike kuNdunankulu KwaZulu - Natal uMnuz Sihle Zikalala .
Isiqinisa idolo nendlela iminxa eyahlukene emphakathini esabele ngayo ekhweleni lokubambisana nohulumeni ekugwemeni umbhedukazwe ngenxa yeCoronavirus .
Kubo bonke esesihlangene nabo kula masonto ambalwa edlule kuhlaluka ukuthi bazimisele ukufaka igxalaba ukuze siyinqobe le mpi - kusukela kubaphathi bamabandla , abaholi bomdabu , abelaphi bendabuko , abemboni yamatekisi , abezibhedlela ezizimele , izinyunyana zabasebenzi nabacoshela izindaba .
Kuyathokozisa nokubona abamabhizinisi adayisa iziphuzo zabadala , abajwayele ukuvakashelwa yizindimbane zamakhasimende , bewulalela umyalelo wokusheshe bavale , ukuze kwehle ukuthelelana ngaleli gciwane .
Siyazi ukuthi lesi akusona isinqumo esilula ngoba sibashaya .
Iqiniso wukuthi uma singashintshi ukwenza kuzolahleka imiphefumulo .
Lo moya wokubambisana esiwubonayo ufakazela esihlale sikusho ukuthi ayikho impi uhulumeni angayinqoba eyedwa , ngaphandle kokubambisana nezinye izinhlaka zomphakathi .
NgoMashi 25 , bonke ongqongqoshe bazobe bephume ngobuningi babo , begasele ezifundeni lapho bewoshampeni khona , ngaphansi kohlelo luka - Operation Sukuma Sakhe , ukuyokhuluma nomphakathi mayelana neCoronavirus .
Le mihlangano ayizukuba nabantu abangaphezu kuka - 100 .
Kufanele omunye nomunye kithina aqale ashintshe ukwenza manje .
Kukhulu ongakuzuza ngokuzijwayeza imikhuba embalwa nje emihle ebukeka imincane kodwa engenza omkhulu umehluko , njengokuthi :  Umboze umlomo noma ikhala ngendololwane ( ufingqe ingalo ) uma ukhwehlela noma uthimula .
Ungavimba nangethishu , bese uyilahla lapho ingeke itholwe womunye .
 Kubalulekile ukuqhela kwabanye abantu okungenani ngegxathu nesigamu ( 1 .
5m ) ukuze bangatheleleki .
 Geza izandla ngamanzi nensipho okungenani imizuzwana ewu - 20 emanzini ahambayo uma ungena ekhaya noma ebhilidini ; ngaphambi kokudla ; noma uma uphuma endlini encane .
Uma kungenzeka , thola isibulala - magciwane .
 Gwema ukuthinta itafula , isihlalo , udonga , isibambo sesicabha , ikhabethe noma udonga olunaleli gciwane bese uthinta umlomo , ikhala noma amehlo , ngoba ingangena kalula kanjalo iCoronavirus .
 Akuphele ukwabelana ngokudla nangamapuleti nezipuni ; nokusebenzisa iziphuzo ngebhodlela elilodwa , nokwabelana ngogwayi ngoba amathe ayabambelela kuwo .
Siyababonga abamabandla asebevumile ukuvala izinkonzo zePhasika , bakhonzele ekhaya , noma kwiTV .
Sicela labo abazoba nezinkonzo ezincane , abasebenzisa ama - microphone emabandleni , nabasakazi , baqikelele ukuthi bayawesula noma basebenzise amagilavu uma bewathinta ngoba nawo angaba yisidleke samathe aneCoronavirus .
Sifisa nokuqondisa izinkoleloze ezikhulunywa abantu abathile mayelana naleli gciwane ukuze isizwe singaduki : Akulona iqiniso ukuthi iCoronavirus ayibahlaseli abantu abamnyama .
Ayikhethi bala ; ihlasela noma wubani osondelana nayo .
Akulona iqiniso ukuthi iCoronavirus iyaphela uma umuntu ethamela ilanga , noma ehlala endaweni eshisa kakhulu .
Akulona iqiniso ukuthi ugologo , noma ezinye izinhlobo zotshwala ziyayelapha iCoronavirus .
Uma singasheshe sikhohlwe yila mampunge , senze lokho okufanele sizosondela ekuziqhelelaniseni negciwane .
Akuyena wonke umuntu onomkhuhlane oneCoronavirus .
Isiqiniseko sokuthi uneCoronavirus noma cha usithola emva kokuthi kuthathwe isampula noma uketshezi ekhaleni ( swab ) luyohlolwa e - laboratory .
Uma uzizwa unomkhuhlane onamandla ngokungajwayelekile , ukhwehlela , uphefumula kanzima , uphethwe yikhanda , kubuhlungu umphimbo namamasela , noma uke wasondelana nomuntu oseke wahlolwa kwatholakala ukuthi unayo iCoronavirus , vakashela umtholampilo ongasekhaya ukuze uxilongwe abezempilo .
Bazokubuza imibuzo mayelana nomlando wakho wakamuva , kuthathwe isampula , uyiswe esibhedlela lapho uzobekwa khona wedwa kusalindwe imiphumela .
Labo abanendawo eyanele ekhaya bazocelwa ukuba bazigqume ekhaya ngesikhathi kusalindwe imiphumela .
Uma imiphumela iveza ukuthi likhona igciwane , uzobe usuthathwa yi - ambulensi eyisipesheli , uyiswe esibhedlela esikhethekile , nesikulungele ukubhekana nabantu abaneCoronavirus .
Sidlulisa ukubonga kubo bonke abasebenzi bezempilo ngesibindi ngomdlandla abawukhombisayo .
Bayinsika ekulweni nalolu bhubhane .
Sinxusa umphakathi ukuthi ungabakhiphi inyumbazana labo abangase batholwe beneCoronavirus , kanjalo nalabo ababahlengayo .
Lesi yisikhathi sokuthi sibambane ngezandla .
Shayela inombolo yamahhala ethi : 0800 029 999 ukuze uthole eminye imininingwane .
* UNomagugu Simelane - Zulu unguNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo KwaZulu - Natal .
I - DA ifuna okukaKhesari kubuyele kuKhesari
MHLELI : Abelungu beDA bathi isikhathi sesifikile " azibuye emasisweni . "
Ilulwane uma lihlezi phansi libukeka njengegundane kodwa kungelona igundane .
Uma lindiza libukeka njengenyoni kodwa lingeyona inyoni .
Uma ungabeka inyoni negundane bese ubuza ukuthi niyamazi lona bayoliphika bonke bathi cha cha cha asimazi .
Ilulwane uma lihlezi phansi alikwazi ukusuka lindize ngoba aliyona inyoni ngokuphelele kufanele lishoshe lize liyokhuphuka ngodonga ukuze lindize .
Ikomkhulu leDA liseNew York kodwa leli qembu eliholwa uMnuz Mmusi Maimane eNingizimu Afrika alikaze limthume emihlanganweni yalo eNew York ngoba unaleli bala okungelona elaseNtshonalanga .
Uyazisisa njengelulwane elizisisa egundaneni nasenyonini .
I - DA uma kufanele ithumele ekomkhulu layo kuba abebala layo hhayi umholi wayo .
Laba belungu bayazi ukuthi uyofika acwaseke ngebala lakhe .
Ubani owayesazi ukuthi kusekhona uMnuz Tony Leon kwiDA .
Akaze aye ndawo kuphela ubebuka le sithunywa abafolose ngaso ukuthi senzani .
Okubuhlungu ukuthi abantu abebezenze amalulwane bahlambalaze isithunzi somuntu omnyama kwabaseNtshonalanga .
Bazoqhubeka nokuthi singothathekile .
Ukwesula kukaMashaba ngibona kuzoba nomthelela ongemuhle kuMaimane othi akuyiwe engqungqutheleni .
UMashaba uzohamba nenqwaba yabantu lokho kusho ukuthi le ndoda izolahlekelwa abayesekayo kuleyo ngqungquthela bese iba yihlaya kwabaseNtshonalanga .
Ngeke kungimangaze ukubona uNkk Hellen Zille noma * Leon engenela esokuphinda ahole leli qembu ngoba lona ubenziwa ihawu lengulube ukuze kuhehwe othathekile .
UNksz Patricia De Lille angazihlomulela kulaba asebesaba ukubuyela ekhaya ngoba ngeke baqhubeke neDA uma abelungu sebemkhiphe ngokusemthethweni uMaimane nabo bonke abahola ezifundazweni njengoMnuz Zwakele Mncwango .
Bafake abebala elimhlophe ngoba bafuna okukaKhesari kubuyele kuKhesari .

nokuthi ukuphazamiseka kwezinhlelo bekungagwemeka ukuba izinhlangothi zombili zikwazile ukuvumelana .

UMkhandlu Wabafundi nabaphathi beNyuvesi babhekene nesimo esinzima kakhulu .
Akugcini nje ngokutholakala kwesisombululo salokhu esibhekene nakho manje kepha kumele futhi siqhamuke nesu lokuhlanganisa izidingo zeNyuvesi zezimali kanye nezidingo ezibalulekile zabafundi esikhathini eside .
Okufanele kushiwo kuqala ilokhu okusobala : udlame nokusabisa kuphambene nenqubo nomqondo wempilo yaseNyuvesi .
Labo abenza lezi zenzo abamele muntu .
Izenzo zokusabisa nezokucekela phansi impahla aziyona ipolitiki yanoma yiluphi uhlobo ; empeleni ziphikisana nepolitiki nokusebenzisa umqondo .
Aziyona indlela yokubhikisha kepha ziyizenzo zobugebengu kanti iNyuvesi izophokophela ukuthi izigilamkhuba zishushiswe .
Siselapho asichithe ulimi lwepolitiki olusetshenziswa budedengu kucashunwa ngokungafanele u - Franz Fanon .
E - Afrika yonke ukuqhakambisa udlame kuka - Fanon osekuvamile kuphikisana nezinjongo ezinhle ; njengoba udlame luholelele kolunye udlame kanti umphumela walokho yiloku esikubona namuhla .
Abasebenzi abazinikele base - UKZN basebenze ngokuzikhandla ukuqinisekisa ukuthi isimo esihle kubona bonke abafundi bethu , ngakho kuyasikhathaza kakhulu ukubona indlela izinto ezenzeka ngayo ezibuyisela emuva .
Indlela yokwenza izinto ngodlame edlangile kwezombusazwe nesilimaze impilo yabantu abaningi eNingizimu Afrika iyindaba yezwe lonke , hhayi i - UKZN kuphela noma ngivuma ukuthi isilimaza kakhulu ngaphezu kwabanye abantu .
Kepha kufanele iphele njengoba icekela phansi wonke umsebenzi omuhle wabangasekho abanikela ngempilo yabo .
Ayamukeleki futhi isenzela phansi sonke manje nangomuso .
AmaNyuvesi kahulumeni ethu aneqhaza elimqoka ukulungisa umonakalo osukela emlandweni wethu .
Ngokunika imiphakathi eyayicindezelwe ithuba lemfundo yaseNyuvesi , senza umsebenzi wesizwe futhi sakha isisekelo somphakathi onokulingana nonekusasa eliqhakazile .
Kepha ayikho iNyuvesi engathintwa yizimo esebenza ngaphansi kwazo .
Lapha sibala konke kusukela esimweni somnotho sezwe nezinjongongqangi zikahulumeni kuze kufinyelele ezimweni zenhlalo yomphakathi wendawo ezithinta umuntu ngamunye nemindeni yonke .
IsiFundazwe iKwaZulu - Natal ( i - KZN ) singesinye sezifundazwe ezinezinga eliphezulu lobubha ezweni , njengoba izinga labantu abadala lingaphezulu kwamaphesenti angama - 60 .
Inselelo yokuntuleka kwemisebenzi , ephezulu ngendlela ethusayo nakubantu abaneziqu , yenza abafundi abaningi baqhubeke bahlale esikoleni ngaphandle kwenhloso etheni , okulandelwa umphumela wokuvalelwa ngaphandle ngenxa yokukweleta noma yokungaphasi okuholela odlameni .
Kanti futhi kuyinto ehlale yenzeka .

0 zibhaliswe zingayikhokhile imali yokubhalisa noma yesikweletu esidala .

Isikweletu sabafundi base - UKZN ekupheleni kukaDisemba wangonyaka wezi - 2019 besiyi - R1 , 7 billion .
Noma kunjalo kepha siqhubekile senza izindlela ( njengokukugunyaza ukubhaliswa ngokwezimali ) okusho ukuthi asikho noyedwa umfundi waseNyuvesi obekufanele akhokhe imali ephelele yesikweletu esidala ngaphambi kokubhalisa .
